//GOD1:937835 coprime_family : "the family #6 indexed by #5 is coprime" | $\operatorname{hcf}(#6_i)=1$
Definition coprime_family :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) ->
set -> (set -> set) -> prop :=
fun K add mul I x =>
highest_common_factor K add mul I x (ring_one K mul).

//GOD1:937835 coprime_elements : "#4 and #5 are coprime in the ring #1" | $\operatorname{hcf}(#4,#5)=1$
Definition coprime_elements :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) ->
set -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul x y =>
coprime_family K add mul 2 (fun i => if i = 0 then x else y).

Theorem god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul -> forall d :e K,
(ring_unit K add mul d
<-> ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul)).
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
let d.
assume hd.
apply iffI.
- assume hUnit.
claim hInverseExists : exists q :e K,
mul q d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d q = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(d :e K)
(exists q :e K,
mul q d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d q = ring_one K mul)
hUnit).
apply hInverseExists.
let q.
assume hqData.
claim hq : q :e K.
exact (andEL
(q :e K)
(mul q d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d q = ring_one K mul) hqData).
claim hqdOne : mul q d = ring_one K mul.
exact (andEL
(mul q d = ring_one K mul)
(mul d q = ring_one K mul)
(andER
(q :e K)
(mul q d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d q = ring_one K mul) hqData)).
exact (andI
(d :e K /\ ring_one K mul :e K)
(exists u :e K, ring_one K mul = mul u d)
(andI (d :e K) (ring_one K mul :e K) hd hOne)
(ex_intro
(fun u => u :e K /\ ring_one K mul = mul u d)
q
(andI
(q :e K) (ring_one K mul = mul q d)
hq (eq_sym (mul q d) (ring_one K mul) hqdOne)))).
- assume hDivides.
claim hQuotientExists : exists q :e K,
ring_one K mul = mul q d.
exact (andER
(d :e K /\ ring_one K mul :e K)
(exists q :e K, ring_one K mul = mul q d) hDivides).
apply hQuotientExists.
let q.
assume hqData.
claim hq : q :e K.
exact (andEL
(q :e K)
(ring_one K mul = mul q d) hqData).
claim hOneEq : ring_one K mul = mul q d.
exact (andER
(q :e K)
(ring_one K mul = mul q d) hqData).
claim hLeft : mul q d = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_sym (ring_one K mul) (mul q d) hOneEq).
claim hRight : mul d q = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul d q) (mul q d) (ring_one K mul)
(hComm d hd q hq) hLeft).
exact (andI
(d :e K)
(exists u :e K,
mul u d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d u = ring_one K mul)
hd
(ex_intro
(fun u => u :e K
/\ (mul u d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d u = ring_one K mul))
q
(andI
(q :e K)
(mul q d = ring_one K mul /\ mul d q = ring_one K mul)
hq
(andI
(mul q d = ring_one K mul)
(mul d q = ring_one K mul) hLeft hRight)))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_theorem1_coprime_characterizations :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(coprime_family K add mul n (fun i => x i)
<-> forall d :e K,
(forall i :e n, ring_divides K mul d (x i)) -> ring_unit K add mul d)
/\ ((forall d :e K,
(forall i :e n, ring_divides K mul d (x i)) -> ring_unit K add mul d)

coprime_family K add mul n y.

(ring_one K mul :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n x
= principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul)) hX).
claim hXIdeal : ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n x

exact (andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n x
= principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul)) hX).
exact (andI

(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y
= principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul))
hOne
(eq_i_tra
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n x)
(principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul))
(eq_sym
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n x)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y) hIdealEq)
hXIdeal)).
claim hReverse : coprime_family K add mul n y ->
coprime_family K add mul n x.
assume hY.

exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y

claim hYIdeal : ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y

exact (andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul n y

Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y d :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
ring_divides K mul d (mul x y) ->
coprime_elements K add mul d x ->
ring_divides K mul d y.
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let d.
assume hd hPID hxne hyne hProduct hCoprime.

exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hAddGroup : group K add.
exact (god1_ring_additive_group K add mul hRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).

(mul (mul v x) y) (mul (mul v q) d)

claim hCoeff : add (mul u y) (mul v q) :e K.
exact (god1_group_law_of_composition K add hAddGroup
(mul u y) huy (mul v q) hvq).
claim hCollect :
add (mul (mul u y) d) (mul (mul v q) d)
= mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d.
exact (eq_sym
(mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d)
(add (mul (mul u y) d) (mul (mul v q) d))
(god1_ring_right_distributive_law K add mul hRing
(mul u y) huy (mul v q) hvq d hd)).
claim hFactorization : y = mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d.
exact (eq_i_tra y
(add (mul (mul u d) y) (mul (mul v x) y))
(mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d)
hyAdd
(eq_i_tra
(add (mul (mul u d) y) (mul (mul v x) y))
(add (mul (mul u y) d) (mul (mul v q) d))
(mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d)
hAddFactored hCollect)).
exact (andI
(d :e K /\ y :e K)
(exists c :e K, y = mul c d)
(andI (d :e K) (y :e K) hd hy)
(ex_intro
(fun c => c :e K /\ y = mul c d)
(add (mul u y) (mul v q))
(andI
(add (mul u y) (mul v q) :e K)
(y = mul (add (mul u y) (mul v q)) d)
hCoeff hFactorization))).
exact h_s31_t2_conclusion.
Qed.

//GOD1:939756 least_common_multiple : "#8 is a least common multiple of family #7" | $#8=\operatorname{lcm}(#7_i)$
Definition least_common_multiple :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) ->
set -> (set -> set) -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul I x m =>
m :e K
/\ {y :e K|forall i :e I, y :e principal_ideal K add mul (x i)}
= principal_ideal K add mul m.

Theorem god1_hcf_quotients_are_coprime_core :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y d xp yp :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add ->
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
x = mul xp d -> y = mul yp d ->
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp.
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let d.
assume hd.
let xp.
assume hxp.
let yp.
assume hyp hPID hxNonzero hHcf hxd hyd.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hAddGroup : group K add.
exact (god1_ring_additive_group K add mul hRing).
claim hdNonzero : d <> ring_zero K add.
assume hdZero.
claim hxZero : x = ring_zero K add.
exact (eq_i_tra x (mul xp d) (ring_zero K add)
hxd
(eq_i_tra
(mul xp d) (mul xp (ring_zero K add)) (ring_zero K add)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul xp z) d (ring_zero K add) hdZero)
(god1_ring_zero_multiplication_right K add mul hRing xp hxp))).
exact (hxNonzero hxZero).
claim hBezoutExists : exists u v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d.
exact (god1_two_element_hcf_bezout_coefficients
K add mul x hx y hy d hd hRing hHcf).
apply hBezoutExists.
let u.
assume huData.
claim hu : u :e K.
exact (andEL
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K, add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d) huData).
claim hVExists : exists v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K, add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d) huData).
apply hVExists.
let v.
assume hvData.
claim hv : v :e K.
exact (andEL
(v :e K)
(add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d) hvData).
claim hBezout : add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d.
exact (andER
(v :e K)
(add (mul u x) (mul v y) = d) hvData).
claim huxp : mul u xp :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing u hu xp hxp).
claim hvyp : mul v yp :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing v hv yp hyp).
claim hCoeff : add (mul u xp) (mul v yp) :e K.
exact (god1_group_law_of_composition K add hAddGroup
(mul u xp) huxp (mul v yp) hvyp).
claim hFirst : mul u x = mul (mul u xp) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul u x) (mul u (mul xp d)) (mul (mul u xp) d)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul u z) x (mul xp d) hxd)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
u hu xp hxp d hd)).
claim hSecond : mul v y = mul (mul v yp) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul v y) (mul v (mul yp d)) (mul (mul v yp) d)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul v z) y (mul yp d) hyd)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
v hv yp hyp d hd)).
claim hFactor :
add (mul u x) (mul v y)
= mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(add (mul u x) (mul v y))
(add (mul (mul u xp) d) (mul (mul v yp) d))
(mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d)
(god1_binary_operation_congruence add
(mul u x) (mul (mul u xp) d)
(mul v y) (mul (mul v yp) d) hFirst hSecond)

(mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d)
(add (mul (mul u xp) d) (mul (mul v yp) d))
(god1_ring_right_distributive_law K add mul hRing
(mul u xp) huxp (mul v yp) hvyp d hd))).
claim hdFactor : d = mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d.
exact (eq_i_tra d
(add (mul u x) (mul v y))
(mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d)
(eq_sym (add (mul u x) (mul v y)) d hBezout)
hFactor).
claim hOneRight : mul d (ring_one K mul) = d.
exact (andEL
(mul d (ring_one K mul) = d)
(mul (ring_one K mul) d = d)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
d hd)).
claim hCommFactor :
mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d
= mul d (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)).
exact ((andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing)
(add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) hCoeff d hd).
claim hCancelEquation :
mul d (ring_one K mul)
= mul d (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul d (ring_one K mul)) d
(mul d (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)))
hOneRight
(eq_i_tra d
(mul (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) d)
(mul d (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)))
hdFactor hCommFactor)).
claim hOneEqCoeff : ring_one K mul = add (mul u xp) (mul v yp).
exact (god1_integral_domain_left_cancel K add mul hIntegral
d hd hdNonzero
(ring_one K mul)
(andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
(add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) hCoeff hCancelEquation).
claim hCoeffOne : add (mul u xp) (mul v yp) = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_sym
(ring_one K mul) (add (mul u xp) (mul v yp)) hOneEqCoeff).
exact (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul xp yp)
(exists a b :e K,
add (mul a xp) (mul b yp) = ring_one K mul)
(god1_s31_theorem1_bezout_coprime_interface
K add mul xp hxp yp hyp hPID)
(ex_intro
(fun a => a :e K /\ exists b :e K,
add (mul a xp) (mul b yp) = ring_one K mul)
u
(andI
(u :e K)
(exists b :e K,
add (mul u xp) (mul b yp) = ring_one K mul)
hu
(ex_intro
(fun b => b :e K
/\ add (mul u xp) (mul b yp) = ring_one K mul)
v
(andI
(v :e K)
(add (mul u xp) (mul v yp) = ring_one K mul)
hv hCoeffOne))))).
Qed.

(mul (mul xp yp) d).

Theorem god1_two_element_hcf_factorization :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
exists d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d.
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hTwoOmega : 2 :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega 2 nat_2).
claim hFamilyMaps : forall i :e 2,
(if i = 0 then x else y) :e K.
let i.
assume hi.
exact (cases_2 i hi
(fun j => (if j = 0 then x else y) :e K)
(mem_eq_substL K x (if 0 = 0 then x else y)
(If_i_1 (0 = 0) x y (eq_ref 0)) hx)
(mem_eq_substL K y (if 1 = 0 then x else y)
(If_i_0 (1 = 0) x y neq_1_0) hy)).
claim hFamily : (fun i :e 2 => if i = 0 then x else y) :e K :^: 2.
exact (lam_Pi 2 (fun i => K)
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) hFamilyMaps).
claim hHcfExists : exists d :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => (fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i) d
/\ (exists coeff :e K :^: 2,
d = module_finitely_supported_sum K add 2
(fun i => mul (coeff i)
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i)))
/\ forall m :e K,
((forall i :e 2, ring_divides K mul m
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i))
<-> ring_divides K mul m d).
exact (god1_hcf_existence_bezout_and_divisor_characterization
K add mul 2 hTwoOmega
(fun i :e 2 => if i = 0 then x else y) hFamily hPID).
apply hHcfExists.
let d.
assume hdData.
claim hd : d :e K.
exact (andEL
(d :e K)
((highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => (fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i) d
/\ exists coeff :e K :^: 2,
d = module_finitely_supported_sum K add 2
(fun i => mul (coeff i)
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i)))
/\ forall m :e K,
((forall i :e 2, ring_divides K mul m
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i))
<-> ring_divides K mul m d))
hdData).
claim hRest :
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => (fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i) d
/\ exists coeff :e K :^: 2,
d = module_finitely_supported_sum K add 2
(fun i => mul (coeff i)
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i)))
/\ forall m :e K,
((forall i :e 2, ring_divides K mul m
((fun j :e 2 => if j = 0 then x else y) i))
<-> ring_divides K mul m d).
exact (andER
(d :e K)
((highest_common_factor K add mul 2

Theorem god1_principal_ideal_unit_multiple :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul -> forall u d :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u ->
principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d)
= principal_ideal K add mul d.
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let u.
assume hu.
let d.
assume hd hUnit.
claim hUD : mul u d :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing u hu d hd).
claim hInverseExists : exists v :e K,
mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K,
mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hUnit).
claim hForward : principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d)
c= principal_ideal K add mul d.
let z.
assume hz.
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun q:set => mul q (mul u d)) z hz
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul d)).
let q.
assume hq hzEq.
claim hQU : mul q u :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing q hq u hu).
claim hRep : mul (mul q u) d :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (ReplI K (fun c:set => mul c d) (mul q u) hQU).
claim hEq : z = mul (mul q u) d.
exact (eq_i_tra z (mul q (mul u d)) (mul (mul q u) d)
hzEq
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
q hq u hu d hd)).
exact (mem_eq_substL
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(mul (mul q u) d) z hEq hRep).
claim hReverse : principal_ideal K add mul d
c= principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d).
let z.
assume hz.
apply hInverseExists.
let v.
assume hvData.
claim hv : v :e K.
exact (andEL
(v :e K)
(mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hvData).
claim hVUOne : mul v u = ring_one K mul.
exact (andEL
(mul v u = ring_one K mul)
(mul u v = ring_one K mul)
(andER
(v :e K)
(mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hvData)).
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun q:set => mul q d) z hz
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d))).
let q.
assume hq hzEq.
claim hQV : mul q v :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing q hq v hv).
claim hQD : mul q d :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing q hq d hd).
claim hRep : mul (mul q v) (mul u d) :e
principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d).
exact (ReplI K (fun c:set => mul c (mul u d)) (mul q v) hQV).
claim hOneRight : mul (mul q d) (ring_one K mul) = mul q d.
exact (andEL
(mul (mul q d) (ring_one K mul) = mul q d)
(mul (ring_one K mul) (mul q d) = mul q d)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall a :e K,
mul a (ring_one K mul) = a /\ mul (ring_one K mul) a = a)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
(mul q d) hQD)).
claim hRepEqQD : mul (mul q v) (mul u d) = mul q d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (mul q v) (mul u d))
(mul (mul q v) (mul d u))
(mul q d)
(f_eq_i (fun a => mul (mul q v) a)
(mul u d) (mul d u) (hComm u hu d hd))
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul q v) (mul d u))
(mul (mul q d) (mul v u))
(mul q d)
(god1_commutative_ring_four_factor_interchange
K add mul hCommRing q hq v hv d hd u hu)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul q d) (mul v u))
(mul (mul q d) (ring_one K mul))
(mul q d)
(f_eq_i (fun a => mul (mul q d) a)
(mul v u) (ring_one K mul) hVUOne)
hOneRight))).
claim hEq : z = mul (mul q v) (mul u d).
exact (eq_i_tra z (mul q d) (mul (mul q v) (mul u d))
hzEq
(eq_sym
(mul (mul q v) (mul u d)) (mul q d) hRepEqQD)).
exact (mem_eq_substL
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d))
(mul (mul q v) (mul u d)) z hEq hRep).
exact (set_ext
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d))
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
hForward hReverse).
Qed.

//GOD1PRF:940600 Remark 1. Since we have the right to replace $d$ by $u d$ and $m$ by $v m$, where $u, v$ are arbitrary units of K, it is clear that the relation $x y=m d$ can only be true if $m$ and $d$ are suitably chosen ; the theorem must be interpreted in this way.
claim h_s31_t3_associate_choices : forall d m u v :e K,

(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul v m).

(eq_i_tra
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y))
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d))
hIdealD
(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u d))
(principal_ideal K add mul d) hPrincipalUD))).
claim hCommonM :
{z :e K|forall i :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (if i = 0 then x else y)}
= principal_ideal K add mul m.
exact (andER
(m :e K)
({z :e K|forall i :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (if i = 0 then x else y)}
= principal_ideal K add mul m)
hLcm).
claim hPrincipalVM : principal_ideal K add mul (mul v m)
= principal_ideal K add mul m.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_unit_multiple
K add mul hCommRing v hv m hm hUnitV).
claim hLcmVM : least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul v m).
exact (andI
(mul v m :e K)
({z :e K|forall i :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (if i = 0 then x else y)}
= principal_ideal K add mul (mul v m))
hVM
(eq_i_tra
{z :e K|forall i :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (if i = 0 then x else y)}
(principal_ideal K add mul m)
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul v m))
hCommonM
(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul v m))
(principal_ideal K add mul m) hPrincipalVM))).
exact (andI
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul u d))
(least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul v m))
hHcfUD hLcmVM).
//GOD1PRF:940855 To prove Theorem 3, put
claim h_s31_t3_factor_by_hcf : exists d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d.
exact (god1_two_element_hcf_factorization
K add mul x hx y hy hPID).
//GOD1PRF:941148 where $z^{\prime}$ is a common multiple of $x^{\prime}$ and $y^{\prime}$, i.e., is a multiple of $m^{\prime}$. Thus the common multiples of $x$ and $y$ are the multiples of $m^{\prime} d$, which is therefore an l.c.m. of $x$ and $y$. Thus we have to prove that $x y=m^{\prime} d$. d, i.e., that
claim h_s31_t3_lcm_from_quotients : exists d m :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m
/\ mul x y = mul m d.
exact h_s31_t3_statement.
//GOD1PRF:941484 Theorem 3 will therefore be a consequence of the following two lemmas:\\
claim h_s31_t3_lemma_reduction :
(forall d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
x = mul xp d -> y = mul yp d ->
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp)
/\ (forall xp yp :e K,
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then xp else yp) (mul xp yp)).
claim hFirstLemma : forall d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
x = mul xp d -> y = mul yp d ->
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp.
let d.
assume hd.
let xp.
assume hxp.
let yp.
assume hyp hHcf hxd hyd.
exact (god1_hcf_quotients_are_coprime_core
K add mul x hx y hy d hd xp hxp yp hyp
hPID hxne hHcf hxd hyd).
claim hSecondLemma : forall xp yp :e K,
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then xp else yp) (mul xp yp).
let xp.
assume hxp.
let yp.
assume hyp hCoprime.
exact (god1_coprime_product_is_lcm_core
K add mul xp hxp yp hyp hPID hCoprime).
exact (andI
(forall d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
x = mul xp d -> y = mul yp d ->
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp)
(forall xp yp :e K,
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then xp else yp) (mul xp yp))
hFirstLemma hSecondLemma).
exact h_s31_t3_lcm_from_quotients.
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma1_quotients_by_hcf_are_coprime :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y d xp yp :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
x = mul xp d -> y = mul yp d ->
coprime_elements K add mul xp yp.
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let d.
assume hd.
let xp.
assume hxp.
let yp.
assume hyp hPID hxne hyne hHcf hxd hyd.
//GOD1PRF:941557 lemma 1. Let $x, y$ be two non-zero elements of K , and let $d$ be a highest common factor of $x$ and $y$. Let $x=x^{\prime} d, y=y^{\prime} d$. Then $x^{\prime}, y^{\prime}$ are coprime.\\
claim h_s31_l1_statement : coprime_elements K add mul xp yp.
exact (god1_hcf_quotients_are_coprime_core
K add mul x hx y hy d hd xp hxp yp hyp
hPID hxne hHcf hxd hyd).
//GOD1PRF:941747 For there exist $u, v \in \mathrm{~K}$ such that $u x+v y=d$, i.e., such that $u x^{\prime}+v y^{\prime}=1$. Hence, by Theorem 1, $x$ and $y$ lare coprime.\\
claim h_s31_l1_theorem1_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall x0 y0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
(coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 x0 y0
<-> exists u0 v0 :e K0,
add0 (mul0 u0 x0) (mul0 v0 y0) = ring_one K0 mul0).
apply god1_s31_theorem1_bezout_coprime_interface.
claim h_s31_l1_bezout_conclusion : coprime_elements K add mul xp yp.
exact h_s31_l1_statement.
exact h_s31_l1_bezout_conclusion.
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma2_product_is_lcm_of_coprime_elements :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
coprime_elements K add mul x y ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul x y).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hCoprime.
//GOD1PRF:941905 lemma 2. If $x, y$ are coprime, then $x y$ is a least common multiple of $x$ and $y$ (in other words, the common multiples of $x$ and $y$ are the multiples of $x y$ ).\\
claim h_s31_l2_statement :
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul x y).
exact (god1_coprime_product_is_lcm_core
K add mul x hx y hy hPID hCoprime).
//GOD1PRF:942075 Let $m$ be a common multiple of $x$ and $y$, and put $m=x z$. Then $y$ divides $x z$; but $y$ is prime to $x$, hence by Theorem $2 y$ divides $z$. Hence $x y$ divides $m$. This completes the proof of Theorem 3.
claim h_s31_l2_theorem2_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 y0 d0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> y0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 (mul0 x0 y0) ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 d0 x0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 y0.
apply god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma.
claim h_s31_l2_common_multiple_conclusion :
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) (mul x y).
exact h_s31_l2_statement.
exact h_s31_l2_common_multiple_conclusion.
Qed.

Theorem god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(coprime_elements K add mul x y
<-> forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d x /\ ring_divides K mul d y ->
ring_unit K add mul d).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hAddGroup : group K add.
exact (god1_ring_additive_group K add mul hRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
apply iffI.
- assume hCoprime.
claim hBezoutExists : exists u v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul x y)
(exists u v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul)
(god1_s31_theorem1_bezout_coprime_interface
K add mul x hx y hy hPID)
hCoprime).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
claim hDX : ring_divides K mul d x.
exact (andEL
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y) hCommon).
claim hDY : ring_divides K mul d y.
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y) hCommon).
claim hQExists : exists q :e K, x = mul q d.
exact (andER
(d :e K /\ x :e K)
(exists q :e K, x = mul q d) hDX).
claim hRExists : exists r :e K, y = mul r d.
exact (andER
(d :e K /\ y :e K)
(exists r :e K, y = mul r d) hDY).
apply hBezoutExists.
let u.
assume huData.
claim hu : u :e K.
exact (andEL
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul)
huData).
claim hVExists : exists v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K,
add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul)
huData).
apply hVExists.
let v.
assume hvData.
claim hv : v :e K.
exact (andEL
(v :e K)
(add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul) hvData).
claim hBezout : add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(v :e K)
(add (mul u x) (mul v y) = ring_one K mul) hvData).
apply hQExists.
let q.
assume hqData.
claim hq : q :e K.
exact (andEL (q :e K) (x = mul q d) hqData).
claim hxd : x = mul q d.
exact (andER (q :e K) (x = mul q d) hqData).
apply hRExists.
let r.
assume hrData.
claim hr : r :e K.
exact (andEL (r :e K) (y = mul r d) hrData).
claim hyd : y = mul r d.
exact (andER (r :e K) (y = mul r d) hrData).
claim huq : mul u q :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing u hu q hq).
claim hvr : mul v r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing v hv r hr).
claim hCoeff : add (mul u q) (mul v r) :e K.
exact (god1_group_law_of_composition K add hAddGroup
(mul u q) huq (mul v r) hvr).
claim hFirst : mul u x = mul (mul u q) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul u x) (mul u (mul q d)) (mul (mul u q) d)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul u z) x (mul q d) hxd)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
u hu q hq d hd)).
claim hSecond : mul v y = mul (mul v r) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul v y) (mul v (mul r d)) (mul (mul v r) d)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul v z) y (mul r d) hyd)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
v hv r hr d hd)).
claim hFactor : add (mul u x) (mul v y)
= mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(add (mul u x) (mul v y))
(add (mul (mul u q) d) (mul (mul v r) d))
(mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d)
(god1_binary_operation_congruence add
(mul u x) (mul (mul u q) d)
(mul v y) (mul (mul v r) d) hFirst hSecond)
(eq_sym
(mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d)
(add (mul (mul u q) d) (mul (mul v r) d))
(god1_ring_right_distributive_law K add mul hRing
(mul u q) huq (mul v r) hvr d hd))).
claim hOneFactor : ring_one K mul
= mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d.
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_one K mul)
(add (mul u x) (mul v y))
(mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d)
(eq_sym
(add (mul u x) (mul v y)) (ring_one K mul) hBezout)
hFactor).
claim hDividesOne : ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul).
exact (andI
(d :e K /\ ring_one K mul :e K)
(exists c :e K, ring_one K mul = mul c d)
(andI (d :e K) (ring_one K mul :e K) hd hOne)
(ex_intro
(fun c => c :e K /\ ring_one K mul = mul c d)
(add (mul u q) (mul v r))
(andI
(add (mul u q) (mul v r) :e K)
(ring_one K mul = mul (add (mul u q) (mul v r)) d)
hCoeff hOneFactor))).
exact (iffER
(ring_unit K add mul d)
(ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one K add mul hCommRing d hd)
hDividesOne).
- assume hEveryCommonUnit.
claim hFactorExists : exists d xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d.
exact (god1_two_element_hcf_factorization
K add mul x hx y hy hPID).
apply hFactorExists.
let d.
assume hdData.
claim hd : d :e K.
exact (andEL
(d :e K)
(exists xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d)
hdData).
claim hXpExists : exists xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d.

(d :e K)
(exists xp yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d)

let xp.
assume hxpData.

exact (andEL
(xp :e K)
(exists yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d)
hxpData).
claim hYpExists : exists yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d.
exact (andER
(xp :e K)
(exists yp :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d /\ y = mul yp d)
hxpData).
apply hYpExists.
let yp.
assume hypData.
claim hyp : yp :e K.
exact (andEL
(yp :e K)
((highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d)
/\ y = mul yp d)
hypData).
claim hFactorData :
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d)
/\ y = mul yp d.

(yp :e K)
((highest_common_factor K add mul 2

/\ y = mul yp d)
hypData).
claim hHcfX :
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d.
exact (andEL
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
/\ x = mul xp d)
(y = mul yp d) hFactorData).
claim hHcf : highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d.
exact (andEL
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d)
(x = mul xp d) hHcfX).
claim hxd : x = mul xp d.
exact (andER
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2

(x = mul xp d) hHcfX).

(y = mul yp d) hFactorData).
claim hDividesX : ring_divides K mul d x.
exact (andI
(d :e K /\ x :e K)

(andI (d :e K) (x :e K) hd hx)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ x = mul q d)
xp (andI (xp :e K) (x = mul xp d) hxp hxd))).

(d :e K /\ y :e K)
(exists q :e K, y = mul q d)
(andI (d :e K) (y :e K) hd hy)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ y = mul q d)

claim hUnitD : ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (hEveryCommonUnit d hd
(andI
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y) hDividesX hDividesY)).

(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y)
= principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (andER
(d :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y)
= principal_ideal K add mul d)
hHcf).
claim hPrincipalD : principal_ideal K add mul d = K.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_of_unit_is_whole_ring

(god1_ring_one_is_unit K add mul hRing)).
exact (andI
(ring_one K mul :e K)

(principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul))

(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul (ring_one K mul))
K hPrincipalOne)))).

Theorem god1_coprime_elements_symmetric :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(coprime_elements K add mul x y
<-> coprime_elements K add mul y x).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID.
claim hXYChar :
coprime_elements K add mul x y
<-> forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d x /\ ring_divides K mul d y ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul x hx y hy hPID).
claim hYXChar :
coprime_elements K add mul y x
<-> forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d y /\ ring_divides K mul d x ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul y hy x hx hPID).
apply iffI.
- assume hXY.
claim hUnitsXY : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d x /\ ring_divides K mul d y ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul x y)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d x /\ ring_divides K mul d y ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
hXYChar hXY).
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul y x)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d y /\ ring_divides K mul d x ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
hYXChar).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
exact (hUnitsXY d hd
(andI
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y)
(andER
(ring_divides K mul d y)
(ring_divides K mul d x) hCommon)
(andEL
(ring_divides K mul d y)
(ring_divides K mul d x) hCommon))).
- assume hYX.
claim hUnitsYX : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d y /\ ring_divides K mul d x ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul y x)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d y /\ ring_divides K mul d x ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
hYXChar hYX).
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul x y)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d x /\ ring_divides K mul d y ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
hXYChar).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
exact (hUnitsYX d hd
(andI
(ring_divides K mul d y)
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(andER
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y) hCommon)
(andEL
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_divides K mul d y) hCommon))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_coprime_elements_right_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall a b c :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
b <> ring_zero K add -> c <> ring_zero K add ->
coprime_elements K add mul a b ->
coprime_elements K add mul a c ->
coprime_elements K add mul a (mul b c).
let K add mul a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb.
let c.
assume hc hPID hbNonzero hcNonzero hCoprimeAB hCoprimeAC.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hProduct : mul b c :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing b hb c hc).
claim hABUnits : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a /\ ring_divides K mul d b ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul a b)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a /\ ring_divides K mul d b ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul a ha b hb hPID)
hCoprimeAB).
claim hACUnits : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a /\ ring_divides K mul d c ->
ring_unit K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul a c)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a /\ ring_divides K mul d c ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul a ha c hc hPID)
hCoprimeAC).
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul a (mul b c))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a
/\ ring_divides K mul d (mul b c) ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul a ha (mul b c) hProduct hPID)).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
claim hDA : ring_divides K mul d a.
exact (andEL
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(ring_divides K mul d (mul b c)) hCommon).
claim hDProduct : ring_divides K mul d (mul b c).
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(ring_divides K mul d (mul b c)) hCommon).
claim hDCoprimeC : coprime_elements K add mul d c.
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul d c)
(forall e :e K,
ring_divides K mul e d /\ ring_divides K mul e c ->
ring_unit K add mul e)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul d hd c hc hPID)).
let e.
assume he hCommonE.
claim hED : ring_divides K mul e d.
exact (andEL
(ring_divides K mul e d)
(ring_divides K mul e c) hCommonE).
claim hEC : ring_divides K mul e c.
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul e d)
(ring_divides K mul e c) hCommonE).
claim hEA : ring_divides K mul e a.
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
e he d hd a ha hED hDA).
exact (hACUnits e he
(andI
(ring_divides K mul e a)
(ring_divides K mul e c) hEA hEC)).
claim hProductComm : mul b c = mul c b.
exact (hComm b hb c hc).
claim hDProductComm : ring_divides K mul d (mul c b).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul d z)
(mul b c) (mul c b) hProductComm hDProduct).
claim hDB : ring_divides K mul d b.
exact (god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma
K add mul c hc b hb d hd hPID
hcNonzero hbNonzero hDProductComm hDCoprimeC).
exact (hABUnits d hd
(andI
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(ring_divides K mul d b) hDA hDB)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_finite_product_nonzero_over_integral_domain :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul ->
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e n, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul n f <> ring_zero K add.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hBase : forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e 0, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e 0, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f <> ring_zero K add.
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero hProductZero.
claim hProductEmpty : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul f).
claim hOneZero : ring_one K mul = ring_zero K add.
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_one K mul)
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f)
(ring_zero K add)
(eq_sym
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f)
(ring_one K mul) hProductEmpty)
hProductZero).
exact ((god1_integral_domain_one_ne_zero K add mul hIntegral) hOneZero).
claim hStep : forall m, nat_p m ->
(forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e m, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e m, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul m f <> ring_zero K add) ->
forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f <> ring_zero K add.
let m.
assume hm hInduction.
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero hProductZero.
claim hmOmega : m :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega m hm).
claim hPrefixMaps : forall i :e m, f i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => hMaps i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixNonzero : forall i :e m,
f i <> ring_zero K add.
exact (fun i hi => hNonzero i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixProductIn : ring_finite_product K add mul m f :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing m
(nat_finite m hm) f hPrefixMaps).
claim hPrefixProductNonzero : ring_finite_product K add mul m f
<> ring_zero K add.
exact (hInduction f hPrefixMaps hPrefixNonzero).
claim hLastIn : f m :e K.
exact (hMaps m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hLastNonzero : f m <> ring_zero K add.
exact (hNonzero m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hSuccessorProduct :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m).
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_natural_successor
K add mul m hmOmega f).
claim hMulZero :
mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m)
= ring_zero K add.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)
(ring_zero K add)
(eq_sym
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
hSuccessorProduct)
hProductZero).
claim hZeroCases :
ring_finite_product K add mul m f = ring_zero K add
\/ f m = ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_zero_product K add mul hIntegral
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f) hPrefixProductIn
(f m) hLastIn hMulZero).
exact (orE
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f = ring_zero K add)
(f m = ring_zero K add) hZeroCases False
hPrefixProductNonzero hLastNonzero).
claim hAll : forall q, nat_p q -> forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e q, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul q f <> ring_zero K add.
exact (nat_ind
(fun q => forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e q, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul q f <> ring_zero K add)
hBase hStep).
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero.
exact (hAll n (omega_nat_p n hn) f hMaps hNonzero).
Qed.

Theorem god1_coprime_elements_finite_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
forall a :e K, forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e n, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e n, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f).
let K add mul.
assume hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
let a.
assume ha.
claim hAOne : coprime_elements K add mul a (ring_one K mul).
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul a (ring_one K mul))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a
/\ ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul) ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul a ha (ring_one K mul) hOne hPID)).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
claim hDividesOne : ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul).
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul)) hCommon).
exact (iffER
(ring_unit K add mul d)
(ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one K add mul hCommRing d hd)
hDividesOne).
claim hBase : forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e 0, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e 0, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e 0, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f).
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero hCoprime.
claim hProductEmpty : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul f).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => coprime_elements K add mul a z)
(ring_one K mul)
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f)
(eq_sym
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f)
(ring_one K mul) hProductEmpty)
hAOne).
claim hStep : forall m, nat_p m ->
(forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e m, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e m, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e m, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f)) ->
forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e ordsucc m, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f).
let m.
assume hm hInduction.
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero hCoprime.
claim hmOmega : m :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega m hm).
claim hPrefixMaps : forall i :e m, f i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => hMaps i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixNonzero : forall i :e m,
f i <> ring_zero K add.
exact (fun i hi => hNonzero i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixCoprime : forall i :e m,
coprime_elements K add mul a (f i).
exact (fun i hi => hCoprime i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixIn : ring_finite_product K add mul m f :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing m
(nat_finite m hm) f hPrefixMaps).
claim hPrefixNonzeroProduct : ring_finite_product K add mul m f
<> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_nonzero_over_integral_domain
K add mul hIntegral m hmOmega f hPrefixMaps hPrefixNonzero).
claim hLastIn : f m :e K.
exact (hMaps m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hLastNonzero : f m <> ring_zero K add.
exact (hNonzero m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hCoprimePrefix : coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f).
exact (hInduction f hPrefixMaps hPrefixNonzero hPrefixCoprime).
claim hCoprimeLast : coprime_elements K add mul a (f m).
exact (hCoprime m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hCoprimeProduct : coprime_elements K add mul a
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m)).
exact (god1_coprime_elements_right_product
K add mul a ha
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f) hPrefixIn
(f m) hLastIn hPID hPrefixNonzeroProduct hLastNonzero
hCoprimePrefix hCoprimeLast).
claim hSuccessorProduct :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m).
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_natural_successor
K add mul m hmOmega f).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => coprime_elements K add mul a z)
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)
(eq_sym
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
hSuccessorProduct)
hCoprimeProduct).
claim hAll : forall q, nat_p q -> forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e q, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e q, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul q f).
exact (nat_ind
(fun q => forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e q, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e q, coprime_elements K add mul a (f i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul a
(ring_finite_product K add mul q f))
hBase hStep).
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
assume hMaps hNonzero hCoprime.
exact (hAll n (omega_nat_p n hn)
f hMaps hNonzero hCoprime).
Qed.

Theorem god1_lcm_extend_family_by_coprime_last :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set, forall p :e K,
f n :e K ->
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
least_common_multiple K add mul n f p ->
coprime_elements K add mul p (f n) ->
least_common_multiple K add mul (ordsucc n) f (mul p (f n)).
let K add mul.
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
let p.
assume hp hLast hPID hPrefixLcm hCoprime.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hProduct : mul p (f n) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
p hp (f n) hLast).
claim hPairLcm : least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then p else f n) (mul p (f n)).
exact (god1_coprime_product_is_lcm_core
K add mul p hp (f n) hLast hPID hCoprime).
claim hPrefixEq :
{z :e K|forall i :e n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
= principal_ideal K add mul p.
exact (andER
(p :e K)
({z :e K|forall i :e n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
= principal_ideal K add mul p)
hPrefixLcm).
claim hPairEq :
{z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}
= principal_ideal K add mul (mul p (f n)).
exact (andER
(mul p (f n) :e K)
({z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}
= principal_ideal K add mul (mul p (f n)))
hPairLcm).
claim hForward :
{z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
c= {z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}.
let z.
assume hzSuccessor.
claim hz : z :e K.
exact (SepE1 K
(fun q => forall i :e ordsucc n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
z hzSuccessor).
claim hAllSuccessor : forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i).
exact (SepE2 K
(fun q => forall i :e ordsucc n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
z hzSuccessor).
claim hAllPrefix : forall i :e n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i).
exact (fun i hi => hAllSuccessor i (ordsuccI1 n i hi)).
claim hzPrefixCommon : z :e
{q :e K|forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}.
exact (SepI K
(fun q => forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
z hz hAllPrefix).
claim hzP : z :e principal_ideal K add mul p.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
{q :e K|forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
(principal_ideal K add mul p) z hPrefixEq hzPrefixCommon).
claim hzLast : z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f n).
exact (hAllSuccessor n (ordsuccI2 n)).
claim hAllPair : forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n).
let j.
assume hj.
exact (cases_2 j hj
(fun k => z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if k = 0 then p else f n))
(mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
(principal_ideal K add mul (if 0 = 0 then p else f n)) z
(f_eq_i (fun q => principal_ideal K add mul q)
p (if 0 = 0 then p else f n)
(eq_sym (if 0 = 0 then p else f n) p
(If_i_1 (0 = 0) p (f n) (eq_ref 0))))
hzP)
(mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul (f n))
(principal_ideal K add mul (if 1 = 0 then p else f n)) z
(f_eq_i (fun q => principal_ideal K add mul q)
(f n) (if 1 = 0 then p else f n)
(eq_sym (if 1 = 0 then p else f n) (f n)
(If_i_0 (1 = 0) p (f n) neq_1_0)))
hzLast)).
exact (SepI K
(fun q => forall j :e 2,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n))
z hz hAllPair).
claim hReverse :
{z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}
c= {z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}.
let z.
assume hzPair.
claim hz : z :e K.
exact (SepE1 K
(fun q => forall j :e 2,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n))
z hzPair).
claim hAllPair : forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n).
exact (SepE2 K
(fun q => forall j :e 2,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n))
z hzPair).
claim hzP : z :e principal_ideal K add mul p.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul (if 0 = 0 then p else f n))
(principal_ideal K add mul p) z
(f_eq_i (fun q => principal_ideal K add mul q)
(if 0 = 0 then p else f n) p
(If_i_1 (0 = 0) p (f n) (eq_ref 0)))
(hAllPair 0 In_0_2)).
claim hzLast : z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f n).
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul (if 1 = 0 then p else f n))
(principal_ideal K add mul (f n)) z
(f_eq_i (fun q => principal_ideal K add mul q)
(if 1 = 0 then p else f n) (f n)
(If_i_0 (1 = 0) p (f n) neq_1_0))
(hAllPair 1 In_1_2)).
claim hzPrefixCommon : z :e
{q :e K|forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
{q :e K|forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)} z
(eq_sym
{q :e K|forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
(principal_ideal K add mul p) hPrefixEq)
hzP).
claim hAllPrefix : forall i :e n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i).
exact (SepE2 K
(fun q => forall i :e n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
z hzPrefixCommon).
claim hAllSuccessor : forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i).
let i.
assume hi.
exact (orE
(i :e n) (i = n) (ordsuccE n i hi)
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
(fun hin => hAllPrefix i hin)
(fun hin => mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul (f n))
(principal_ideal K add mul (f i)) z
(f_eq_i (fun q => principal_ideal K add mul q)
(f n) (f i)
(f_eq_i f n i (eq_sym i n hin)))
hzLast)).
exact (SepI K
(fun q => forall i :e ordsucc n,
q :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i))
z hz hAllSuccessor).
claim hCommonEq :
{z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
= {z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}.
exact (set_ext
{z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
{z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}
hForward hReverse).
exact (andI
(mul p (f n) :e K)
({z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
= principal_ideal K add mul (mul p (f n)))
hProduct
(eq_i_tra
{z :e K|forall i :e ordsucc n,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul (f i)}
{z :e K|forall j :e 2,
z :e principal_ideal K add mul
(if j = 0 then p else f n)}
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul p (f n)))
hCommonEq hPairEq)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_pairwise_coprime_finite_product_is_lcm_core :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e n, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i j :e n, i <> j ->
coprime_elements K add mul (f i) (f j)) ->
least_common_multiple K add mul n f
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f).
let K add mul.
claim hBase : forall f:set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(forall i :e 0, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e 0, f i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i j :e 0, i <> j ->
coprime_elements K add mul (f i) (f j)) ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 0 f
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f).
let f.
assume hPID hMaps hNonzero hPairwise.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->

Theorem god1_s31_theorem4_pairwise_coprime_product_is_lcm :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(forall i :e n, x i <> ring_zero K add) ->

(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)).

let n.

let x.

//GOD1PRF:942329 THEOREM 4. Let $x_{1}, \ldots, x_{n}$ be non-zero elements of K which are coprime in pairs. Then $x_{1} \ldots x_{n}$ is a least common multiple of $x_{1}, \ldots, x_{n}$.

(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)).

exact (god1_pairwise_coprime_finite_product_is_lcm_core
K add mul n hn (fun i => x i) hPID
hMaps hNonzero hPairwise).
//GOD1PRF:942502 For $n=2$, this is Lemma 2. We may therefore proceed by induction, and assume that the theorem is true for a product of $n-1$ factors.

forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 y0 :e K0,

(fun i => if i = 0 then x0 else y0) (mul0 x0 y0).
apply god1_s31_lemma2_product_is_lcm_of_coprime_elements.

n = ordsucc m ->

(ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => x i)).

//GOD1PRF:942638 We shall first show, by induction on $n$, that $x_{n}$ is prime to the product $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-1}$. If $n=2$, this is the hypothesis that the $x_{i}$ are coprime in pairs. Suppose then that we have proved that $x_{n}$ is prime to $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-2}$, and let $d$ be a common divisor of $x_{n}$ and $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-1}$. Since $d$ divides $x_{n}$, which is prime to $x_{n-1}$, it is clear that $d$ is prime to $x_{n-1}$. But $d$ divides $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-1}$, therefore (Theorem 2) $d$ divides $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-2}$. Now $x_{n}$ and $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-2}$ are coprime, by the inductive hypothesis; hence $d$ is a unit, which proves our assertion.
claim h_s31_t4_theorem2_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 y0 d0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> y0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 (mul0 x0 y0) ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 d0 x0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 y0.
apply god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma.
claim h_s31_t4_last_factor_coprime : forall m :e omega,
n = ordsucc m ->
coprime_elements K add mul
(x m)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => x i)).

assume hm hnm.
claim hPrefixToN : forall i :e m, i :e n.
let i.
assume hi.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(ordsucc m) n i
(eq_sym n (ordsucc m) hnm)
(ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hLastInN : m :e n.

(ordsucc m) n m
(eq_sym n (ordsucc m) hnm)
(ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hLastIn : x m :e K.
exact (ap_Pi n (fun q => K) x m hx hLastInN).
claim hPrefixMaps : forall i :e m, x i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => ap_Pi n (fun q => K) x i hx
(hPrefixToN i hi)).
claim hPrefixNonzero : forall i :e m,
x i <> ring_zero K add.
exact (fun i hi => hNonzero i (hPrefixToN i hi)).
claim hLastCoprimeEach : forall i :e m,
coprime_elements K add mul (x m) (x i).

K add mul hPID (x m) hLastIn m hm

//GOD1PRF:943295 We can now prove Theorem 4 by induction on $n$. Let $m$ be a common multiple of the $x_{i}$; assuming the truth of the theorem for a product of $n-1$ factors, we see that $m$ is a multiple of $x_{1} \ldots x_{n-1}$ and also a multiple of $x_{n}$. But we have just seen that these two elements of K are coprime ; hence, by Lemma 2, $m$ is a multiple of their product, i.e., a multiple of $x_{1} \ldots x_{n}$.\\
claim h_s31_t4_lemma2_second_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 y0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 x0 y0 ->

(fun i => if i = 0 then x0 else y0) (mul0 x0 y0).
apply god1_s31_lemma2_product_is_lcm_of_coprime_elements.

least_common_multiple K add mul n (fun i => x i)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)).
exact h_s31_t4_statement.
exact h_s31_t4_conclusion.
Qed.

Theorem god1_commutative_ring_left_ideal_is_two_sided :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul -> forall I,
left_ideal K add mul I -> two_sided_ideal K add mul I.
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let I.
assume hLeft.
claim hLeftPrefix :
((ring K add mul /\ I c= K) /\ subgroup K add I).
exact (andEL
((ring K add mul /\ I c= K) /\ subgroup K add I)
(forall a :e K, forall x :e I, mul a x :e I)
hLeft).
claim hSubset : I c= K.
exact (andER
(ring K add mul)
(I c= K)
(andEL
(ring K add mul /\ I c= K)
(subgroup K add I) hLeftPrefix)).
claim hLeftClosed : forall a :e K, forall x :e I,
mul a x :e I.
exact (andER
((ring K add mul /\ I c= K) /\ subgroup K add I)
(forall a :e K, forall x :e I, mul a x :e I)
hLeft).
claim hRightClosed : forall a :e K, forall x :e I,
mul x a :e I.
let a.
assume ha.
let x.
assume hx.
claim hax : mul a x :e I.
exact (hLeftClosed a ha x hx).
exact (mem_eq_substL I (mul a x) (mul x a)
(hComm x (hSubset x hx) a ha) hax).
claim hRight : right_ideal K add mul I.
exact (andI
((ring K add mul /\ I c= K) /\ subgroup K add I)
(forall a :e K, forall x :e I, mul x a :e I)
hLeftPrefix hRightClosed).
exact (andI
(left_ideal K add mul I)
(right_ideal K add mul I)
hLeft hRight).
Qed.

Theorem god1_principal_ideal_domain_left_noetherian :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
left_noetherian_ring K add mul.
let K add mul.
assume hPID.

(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,

hPID).

exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hPrincipal : forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (andER
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hIdealsFinite : forall I,
left_ideal K add mul I ->
finitely_generated_module K add mul I add mul.
let I.
assume hLeft.
claim hTwoSided : two_sided_ideal K add mul I.
exact (god1_commutative_ring_left_ideal_is_two_sided
K add mul hCommRing I hLeft).
claim hGeneratorExists : exists a :e K,
I = principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (hPrincipal I hTwoSided).
apply hGeneratorExists.
let a.
assume haData.
claim ha : a :e K.
exact (andEL
(a :e K)
(I = principal_ideal K add mul a) haData).
claim hIdealEq : I = principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (andER
(a :e K)
(I = principal_ideal K add mul a) haData).
claim hPrincipalFinite : finitely_generated_module K add mul
(principal_ideal K add mul a) add mul.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_finitely_generated_module
K add mul hCommRing a ha).
exact (god1_finitely_generated_module_carrier_eq_subst
K add mul I (principal_ideal K add mul a) add mul

(ring K add mul)
(forall I, left_ideal K add mul I ->
finitely_generated_module K add mul I add mul)
hRing hIdealsFinite).
Qed.

//GOD1:943756 extremal_element : "#4 is an extremal element of the principal ideal domain #1" | $#4\text{ is extremal}$
Definition extremal_element :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul p =>
p :e K
/\ p <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p)
/\ forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.

//GOD1:947164 factorization_into_extremals : "#4 is a product of a unit and finitely many extremal elements" | $#4=u\prod_i p_i$
Definition factorization_into_extremals :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul x =>
exists n :e omega, exists u :e K, exists p :e K :^: n,
ring_unit K add mul u
/\ (forall i :e n, extremal_element K add mul (p i))
/\ x = mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => p i)).

Theorem god1_extremal_has_factorization_into_extremals :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall q :e K,
extremal_element K add mul q ->
factorization_into_extremals K add mul q.
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
claim hUnitOne : ring_unit K add mul (ring_one K mul).
exact (god1_ring_one_is_unit K add mul hRing).
claim hFactorOne : factorization_into_extremals K add mul
(ring_one K mul).
exact (god1_unit_has_factorization_into_extremals
K add mul hRing (ring_one K mul) hOne hUnitOne).
let q.
assume hq hExtremal.
claim hAppended : factorization_into_extremals K add mul
(mul (ring_one K mul) q).
exact (god1_factorization_into_extremals_append_extremal
K add mul hRing (ring_one K mul) hOne q hq
hFactorOne hExtremal).
claim hLeftIdentity : mul (ring_one K mul) q = q.
exact (andER
(mul q (ring_one K mul) = q)
(mul (ring_one K mul) q = q)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
q hq)).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => factorization_into_extremals K add mul z)
(mul (ring_one K mul) q) q hLeftIdentity hAppended).
Qed.

(n :e omega)

Theorem god1_nonextremal_nonunit_splits_into_two_nonunits :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall a :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
a <> ring_zero K add ->
not (ring_unit K add mul a) ->
not (extremal_element K add mul a) ->
exists b c :e K,
(a = mul b c
/\ (not (ring_unit K add mul b)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul c)))
/\ (b <> ring_zero K add /\ c <> ring_zero K add).
let K add mul a.
assume ha hPID haNonzero hNonunitA hNonextremal.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hNotDivisorCondition : not (forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
assume hDivisorCondition.
claim hExtremal : extremal_element K add mul a.
exact (andI
((a :e K /\ a <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul a))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a)
(andI
(a :e K /\ a <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul a))
(andI
(a :e K) (a <> ring_zero K add) ha haNonzero)
hNonunitA)
hDivisorCondition).
exact (hNonextremal hExtremal).
claim hWitnessRaw : exists d, not (d :e K ->
ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
exact (not_all_ex_demorgan_i
(fun d => d :e K ->
ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a)
hNotDivisorCondition).
apply hWitnessRaw.
let d.
assume hNotImpD.
claim hd : d :e K.
exact (orE
(d :e K) (d /:e K) (xm (d :e K))
(d :e K)
(fun hdK => hdK)
(fun hdNot => FalseE
(hNotImpD
(fun hdK => FalseE (hdNot hdK)
(ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a)))
(d :e K))).
claim hNotRest : not (ring_divides K mul d a ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
assume hRest.
exact (hNotImpD (fun hdK => hRest)).
claim hDivides : ring_divides K mul d a.
exact (orE
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(not (ring_divides K mul d a))
(xm (ring_divides K mul d a))
(ring_divides K mul d a)
(fun hD => hD)
(fun hNotD => FalseE
(hNotRest
(fun hD => FalseE (hNotD hD)
(ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a)))
(ring_divides K mul d a))).
claim hNotChoices : not (
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
assume hChoices.
exact (hNotRest (fun hD => hChoices)).
claim hChoiceNegations :
not (ring_unit K add mul d)
/\ not (exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
exact (not_or_and_demorgan
(ring_unit K add mul d)
(exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a)
hNotChoices).
claim hNonunitD : not (ring_unit K add mul d).
exact (andEL
(not (ring_unit K add mul d))
(not (exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a))
hChoiceNegations).
claim hNoAssociate : not (exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a).
exact (andER
(not (ring_unit K add mul d))
(not (exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u a))
hChoiceNegations).
claim hQExists : exists q :e K, a = mul q d.
exact (andER
(d :e K /\ a :e K)
(exists q :e K, a = mul q d) hDivides).
apply hQExists.
let q.
assume hqData.
claim hq : q :e K.
exact (andEL (q :e K) (a = mul q d) hqData).
claim haEq : a = mul q d.
exact (andER (q :e K) (a = mul q d) hqData).
claim hNonunitQ : not (ring_unit K add mul q).
assume hUnitQ.
claim hInverseSpec : reflection K mul (ring_one K mul)
q (ring_inverse K add mul q).
exact (god1_ring_inverse_specification K add mul q hUnitQ).
claim hInvPrefix :
ring_inverse K add mul q :e K
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q = ring_one K mul.
exact (andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul q :e K
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q = ring_one K mul)
(mul q (ring_inverse K add mul q) = ring_one K mul)
hInverseSpec).
claim hInv : ring_inverse K add mul q :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul q :e K)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q = ring_one K mul)
hInvPrefix).
claim hInvQ : mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q
= ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(ring_inverse K add mul q :e K)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q = ring_one K mul)
hInvPrefix).
claim hInvUnit : ring_unit K add mul (ring_inverse K add mul q).
exact (god1_ring_inverse_is_unit K add mul hRing q hUnitQ).
claim hOneLeft : mul (ring_one K mul) d = d.
exact (andER
(mul d (ring_one K mul) = d)
(mul (ring_one K mul) d = d)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
d hd)).
claim hAssociateEq : d = mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) a.
exact (eq_sym
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) a) d
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) a)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) (mul q d)) d
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) z)
a (mul q d) haEq)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) (mul q d))
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul q) q) d) d
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul q) hInv q hq d hd)

Theorem god1_nonunit_cofactor_strictly_enlarges_principal_ideal :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul -> forall a b c :e K,
a = mul b c ->
b <> ring_zero K add ->
not (ring_unit K add mul c) ->
principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul b
/\ principal_ideal K add mul b <> principal_ideal K add mul a.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb.
let c.
assume hc haEq hbNonzero hNonunitC.
claim hSubset : principal_ideal K add mul a
c= principal_ideal K add mul b.
let z.
assume hzA.
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun r:set => mul r a) z hzA
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul b)).
let r.
assume hr hzEq.
claim hRC : mul r c :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing r hr c hc).
claim hRepresentative : mul (mul r c) b
:e principal_ideal K add mul b.
exact (ReplI K (fun q:set => mul q b) (mul r c) hRC).
claim hzTarget : z = mul (mul r c) b.
exact (eq_i_tra z (mul r a) (mul (mul r c) b)
hzEq
(eq_i_tra
(mul r a) (mul r (mul b c)) (mul (mul r c) b)
(f_eq_i (fun q => mul r q) a (mul b c) haEq)
(eq_i_tra
(mul r (mul b c)) (mul r (mul c b)) (mul (mul r c) b)
(f_eq_i (fun q => mul r q)
(mul b c) (mul c b) (hComm b hb c hc))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
r hr c hc b hb)))).
exact (mem_eq_substL
(principal_ideal K add mul b)
(mul (mul r c) b) z hzTarget hRepresentative).
claim hStrict : principal_ideal K add mul b
<> principal_ideal K add mul a.
assume hIdealsEq.
claim hbInB : b :e principal_ideal K add mul b.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_contains_generator K add mul hRing b hb).
claim hbInA : b :e principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul b)
(principal_ideal K add mul a) b
hIdealsEq
hbInB).
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun r:set => mul r a) b hbInA False).
let r.
assume hr hbEq.
claim hRC : mul r c :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing r hr c hc).
claim hbFactorEq : b = mul b (mul r c).
exact (eq_i_tra b (mul r a) (mul b (mul r c))
hbEq
(eq_i_tra
(mul r a) (mul r (mul b c)) (mul b (mul r c))
(f_eq_i (fun q => mul r q) a (mul b c) haEq)
(eq_i_tra
(mul r (mul b c)) (mul (mul r b) c) (mul b (mul r c))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
r hr b hb c hc)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul r b) c) (mul (mul b r) c)
(mul b (mul r c))
(f_eq_i (fun q => mul q c)
(mul r b) (mul b r) (hComm r hr b hb))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative_reverse
K add mul hRing b hb r hr c hc))))).
claim hIdentityData : ring_one K mul :e K
/\ forall q :e K,
mul q (ring_one K mul) = q /\ mul (ring_one K mul) q = q.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification
K add mul hRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall q :e K,
mul q (ring_one K mul) = q /\ mul (ring_one K mul) q = q)
hIdentityData).
claim hbOne : mul b (ring_one K mul) = b.
exact (andEL
(mul b (ring_one K mul) = b)
(mul (ring_one K mul) b = b)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall q :e K,
mul q (ring_one K mul) = q /\ mul (ring_one K mul) q = q)
hIdentityData) b hb)).
claim hCancelEq : mul b (ring_one K mul) = mul b (mul r c).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul b (ring_one K mul)) b (mul b (mul r c))
hbOne hbFactorEq).
claim hOneEqRC : ring_one K mul = mul r c.
exact (god1_integral_domain_left_cancel K add mul hIntegral
b hb hbNonzero (ring_one K mul) hOne (mul r c) hRC hCancelEq).
claim hRCOne : mul r c = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_sym (ring_one K mul) (mul r c) hOneEqRC).
claim hCROne : mul c r = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra (mul c r) (mul r c) (ring_one K mul)
(hComm c hc r hr) hRCOne).
claim hUnitC : ring_unit K add mul c.
exact (andI
(c :e K)
(exists q :e K,
mul q c = ring_one K mul /\ mul c q = ring_one K mul)
hc
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K
/\ (mul q c = ring_one K mul /\ mul c q = ring_one K mul))
r
(andI
(r :e K)
(mul r c = ring_one K mul /\ mul c r = ring_one K mul)
hr
(andI
(mul r c = ring_one K mul)
(mul c r = ring_one K mul)
hRCOne hCROne)))).
exact (hNonunitC hUnitC).
exact (andI
(principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul b)
(principal_ideal K add mul b <> principal_ideal K add mul a)
hSubset hStrict).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma3_maximal_member_interface :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall X,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
X <> 0 ->
(forall I :e X, two_sided_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I :e X, forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I.
let K add mul X.
assume hPID hXNonempty hIdeals.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hNoetherian : left_noetherian_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_domain_left_noetherian
K add mul hPID).
claim hConditions :
(forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, left_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
stationary_sequence_of_sets K A)
/\ (forall F,
F <> 0 -> (forall I :e F, left_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I, maximal_element_by_inclusion K F I).
exact (iffEL
(left_noetherian_ring K add mul)
((forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, left_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
stationary_sequence_of_sets K A)
/\ (forall F,
F <> 0 -> (forall I :e F, left_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I, maximal_element_by_inclusion K F I))
(god1_s18_theorem4_noetherian_chain_conditions
K add mul hRing)
hNoetherian).
claim hMaximalFamilies : forall F,
F <> 0 -> (forall I :e F, left_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I, maximal_element_by_inclusion K F I.
exact (andER
(forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, left_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
stationary_sequence_of_sets K A)
(forall F,
F <> 0 -> (forall I :e F, left_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I, maximal_element_by_inclusion K F I)
hConditions).
claim hLeftIdeals : forall I :e X, left_ideal K add mul I.
exact (fun I hI => andEL
(left_ideal K add mul I)
(right_ideal K add mul I)
(hIdeals I hI)).
claim hMaximalExists : exists I,
maximal_element_by_inclusion K X I.
exact (hMaximalFamilies X hXNonempty hLeftIdeals).
apply hMaximalExists.
let I.
assume hMaximal.
claim hMaximalPrefix : X c= Power K /\ I :e X.
exact (andEL
(X c= Power K /\ I :e X)
(forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I)
hMaximal).
claim hI : I :e X.
exact (andER
(X c= Power K)
(I :e X) hMaximalPrefix).
claim hMaximalProperty : forall J :e X,
I c= J -> J = I.
exact (andER
(X c= Power K /\ I :e X)
(forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I)
hMaximal).
exact (ex_intro
(fun A => A :e X /\ forall J :e X, A c= J -> J = A)
I
(andI
(I :e X)
(forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I)
hI hMaximalProperty)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_remark2_pid_maximal_ideal_family_interface :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall X,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
X <> 0 ->
(forall I :e X, two_sided_ideal K add mul I) ->

Definition god1_nonfactorable_principal_ideal_family :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) -> set :=
fun K add mul =>
{I :e Power K|exists a :e K,
(a <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul a))
/\ I = principal_ideal K add mul a}.
