(b <> ring_zero K add) (c <> ring_zero K add) hNonzeros).
claim hcNonzero : c <> ring_zero K add.
exact (andER
(b <> ring_zero K add) (c <> ring_zero K add) hNonzeros).
claim hStrictB :
principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul b
/\ principal_ideal K add mul b <> principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (god1_nonunit_cofactor_strictly_enlarges_principal_ideal
K add mul hIntegral a ha b hb c hc haEq hbNonzero hNonunitC).
claim hASubB : principal_ideal K add mul a
c= principal_ideal K add mul b.
exact (andEL
(principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul b)
(principal_ideal K add mul b <> principal_ideal K add mul a)
hStrictB).
claim hBNotEqA : principal_ideal K add mul b
<> principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (andER
(principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul b)
(principal_ideal K add mul b <> principal_ideal K add mul a)
hStrictB).
claim haEqCB : a = mul c b.
exact (eq_i_tra a (mul b c) (mul c b)
haEq (hComm b hb c hc)).
claim hStrictC :
principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul c
/\ principal_ideal K add mul c <> principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (god1_nonunit_cofactor_strictly_enlarges_principal_ideal
K add mul hIntegral a ha c hc b hb haEqCB hcNonzero hNonunitB).
claim hASubC : principal_ideal K add mul a
c= principal_ideal K add mul c.
exact (andEL
(principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul c)
(principal_ideal K add mul c <> principal_ideal K add mul a)
hStrictC).
claim hCNotEqA : principal_ideal K add mul c
<> principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (andER
(principal_ideal K add mul a c= principal_ideal K add mul c)
(principal_ideal K add mul c <> principal_ideal K add mul a)
hStrictC).
claim hFactorB : factorization_into_extremals K add mul b.
apply (orE
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul b)
(not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul b))
(xm (factorization_into_extremals K add mul b))
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul b)).
exact (fun hFactor => hFactor).
assume hNotFactorB.
claim hPrincipalBBad : principal_ideal K add mul b :e
god1_nonfactorable_principal_ideal_family K add mul.
exact (SepI (Power K)
(fun J => exists y :e K,
(y <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul y))
/\ J = principal_ideal K add mul y)
(principal_ideal K add mul b)
(PowerI K (principal_ideal K add mul b)
(hPrincipalSubsets b hb))
(ex_intro
(fun y => y :e K
/\ ((y <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul y))
/\ principal_ideal K add mul b
= principal_ideal K add mul y))
b
(andI
(b :e K)
((b <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul b))
/\ principal_ideal K add mul b
= principal_ideal K add mul b)
hb
(andI
(b <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul b))
(principal_ideal K add mul b
= principal_ideal K add mul b)
(andI
(b <> ring_zero K add)
(not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul b))
hbNonzero hNotFactorB)
(eq_ref (principal_ideal K add mul b)))))).
claim hISubB : I c= principal_ideal K add mul b.
let z.
assume hzI.
exact (hASubB z
(mem_eq_set_subst I (principal_ideal K add mul a)
z hIEq hzI)).
claim hBEqualsI : principal_ideal K add mul b = I.
exact (hMaximal
(principal_ideal K add mul b) hPrincipalBBad hISubB).
claim hBEqualsA : principal_ideal K add mul b
= principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (eq_i_tra
(principal_ideal K add mul b) I
(principal_ideal K add mul a) hBEqualsI hIEq).
exact (FalseE (hBNotEqA hBEqualsA)
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul b)).
claim hFactorC : factorization_into_extremals K add mul c.
apply (orE
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul c)
(not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul c))
(xm (factorization_into_extremals K add mul c))
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul c)).
exact (fun hFactor => hFactor).
assume hNotFactorC.
claim hPrincipalCBad : principal_ideal K add mul c :e
god1_nonfactorable_principal_ideal_family K add mul.
exact (SepI (Power K)
(fun J => exists y :e K,
(y <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul y))
/\ J = principal_ideal K add mul y)
(principal_ideal K add mul c)
(PowerI K (principal_ideal K add mul c)
(hPrincipalSubsets c hc))
(ex_intro
(fun y => y :e K
/\ ((y <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul y))
/\ principal_ideal K add mul c
= principal_ideal K add mul y))
c
(andI
(c :e K)
((c <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul c))
/\ principal_ideal K add mul c
= principal_ideal K add mul c)

(andI
(c <> ring_zero K add
/\ not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul c))
(principal_ideal K add mul c
= principal_ideal K add mul c)
(andI
(c <> ring_zero K add)
(not (factorization_into_extremals K add mul c))
hcNonzero hNotFactorC)
(eq_ref (principal_ideal K add mul c)))))).
claim hISubC : I c= principal_ideal K add mul c.
let z.
assume hzI.
exact (hASubC z
(mem_eq_set_subst I (principal_ideal K add mul a)
z hIEq hzI)).
claim hCEqualsI : principal_ideal K add mul c = I.
exact (hMaximal
(principal_ideal K add mul c) hPrincipalCBad hISubC).

= principal_ideal K add mul a.

(principal_ideal K add mul c) I
(principal_ideal K add mul a) hCEqualsI hIEq).
exact (FalseE (hCNotEqA hCEqualsA)
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul c)).
claim hFactorBC : factorization_into_extremals K add mul (mul b c).
exact (god1_factorization_into_extremals_product
K add mul hCommRing b hb c hc hFactorB hFactorC).
claim hFactorA : factorization_into_extremals K add mul a.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => factorization_into_extremals K add mul z)
(mul b c) a (eq_sym a (mul b c) haEq) hFactorBC).
exact (FalseE (hNotFactorA hFactorA)
(factorization_into_extremals K add mul x)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_theorem5_existence_of_extremal_factorization :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall x :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> factorization_into_extremals K add mul x.
let K add mul x.
assume hx hPID hxne.
//GOD1PRF:944429 theorem 5. Let K be a principal ideal domain. Then every non-zero element of K is the product of a unit and extremal elements of K .
claim h_s31_t5_statement : factorization_into_extremals K add mul x.
exact (god1_pid_nonzero_factorization_by_maximal_bad_ideal
K add mul x hx hPID hxne).
//GOD1PRF:944563 In other words : every $x \in \mathrm{~K}$ which is neither zero nor a unit is a product of extremal elements of K . (A unit cannot be a product of extremal elements, for the divisors of a unit are units and therefore can never be extremal).
claim h_s31_t5_nonunit_factorization :
not (ring_unit K add mul x) -> factorization_into_extremals K add mul x.
exact (fun hNonunit => h_s31_t5_statement).
//GOD1PRF:944806 To prove Theorem 5, we remark first that a principal ideal domain is a fortiori Noetherian: all its ideals are finitely generated. Consequently (§ 18, Theorem 4, or Remark 2 below) we have the following result:\\
claim h_s31_t5_s18_theorem4_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
ring K0 add0 mul0 ->
(left_noetherian_ring K0 add0 mul0
<-> (forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K0 A ->
(forall n0 :e omega, left_ideal K0 add0 mul0 (A n0)) ->
stationary_sequence_of_sets K0 A)
/\ (forall F,
F <> 0 -> (forall I :e F, left_ideal K0 add0 mul0 I) ->
exists I, maximal_element_by_inclusion K0 F I)).
apply god1_s18_theorem4_noetherian_chain_conditions.
claim h_s31_t5_remark2_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall X0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
X0 <> 0 ->
(forall I :e X0, two_sided_ideal K0 add0 mul0 I) ->
exists I :e X0, forall J :e X0, I c= J -> J = I.
apply god1_s31_remark2_pid_maximal_ideal_family_interface.
//GOD1PRF:945243 We shall use this result to prove Theorem 5 by reductio ad absurdum. Let X be the set of all ideals $\mathrm{I}=(x)$ of K such that $x$ is a non-zero element of K which cannot be written as a product of a unit and extremal elements of K ; then we have to show that X is empty. Suppose then that X is not empty; then by Lemma 3, X contains a maximal element, say (a). The element $a$ cannot be written as a product of a unit and extremal elements, hence is neither a unit nor extremal. Hence we may write $a=b c$, where neither $b$ nor $c$ is a unit ; and this means that the ideals (b) and (c) contain (a) strictly. Hence, by the maximality of (a), we see that (b) and (c) do not belong to X, i.e., Theorem 5 is true for $b$ and $c$. But then it is clearly also true for their product $a$, contrary to the hypothesis that $(a) \in \mathrm{X}$. This contradiction completes the proof.
claim h_s31_t5_lemma3_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall X0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
X0 <> 0 ->
(forall I :e X0, two_sided_ideal K0 add0 mul0 I) ->
exists I :e X0, forall J :e X0, I c= J -> J = I.
apply god1_s31_lemma3_maximal_member_interface.
claim h_s31_t5_maximal_counterexample_contradiction :
factorization_into_extremals K add mul x.
exact (god1_pid_nonzero_factorization_by_maximal_bad_ideal
K add mul x hx hPID hxne).
exact h_s31_t5_statement.
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma3_maximal_member_of_nonempty_ideal_family :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall X,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
X <> 0 ->
(forall I :e X, two_sided_ideal K add mul I) ->
exists I :e X, forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I.
let K add mul X.
assume hPID hX hIdeals.
//GOD1PRF:945020 lemma 3. Let X be a non-empty set of ideals of a principal ideal ring K . Then X has at least one maximal element : that is, there exists $\mathrm{I} \in \mathrm{X}$ not contained in any other $\mathrm{J} \in \mathrm{X}$.
claim h_s31_l3_statement :
exists I :e X, forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I.
exact (god1_s31_lemma3_maximal_member_interface
K add mul X hPID hX hIdeals).
//GOD1PRF:946923 It is perhaps worth while to remind the reader that in any event a direct proof of Lemma 3 is extremely simple, and runs as follows. If Lemma 3 were false, we should be able, starting with an arbitrary ideal $I_{1} \in X$, to construct an $I_{2} \in X$ which strictly contained $I_{1}$, then an $\mathrm{I}_{3} \in \mathrm{X}$ strictly containing $\mathrm{I}_{2}$, and so on indefinitely. To obtain the desired contradiction it is therefore enough to show that all increasing sequences
claim h_s31_l3_increasing_chain_reduction :
forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, two_sided_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
stationary_sequence_of_sets K A.
claim hNoetherian : left_noetherian_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_domain_left_noetherian
K add mul hPID).
let A.
assume hIncreasing hChainIdeals.
claim hLeftIdeals : forall n :e omega,
left_ideal K add mul (A n).
exact (fun n hn => andEL
(left_ideal K add mul (A n))
(right_ideal K add mul (A n))
(hChainIdeals n hn)).
exact (god1_left_noetherian_increasing_ideal_chain_stationary
K add mul hNoetherian A hIncreasing hLeftIdeals).
//GOD1PRF:947508 of ideals of K are stationary, in other words that there exists an integer $r$ such that
claim h_s31_l3_stationary_index : forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, two_sided_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
exists r :e omega, forall n :e omega, r c= n -> A n = A r.
let A.
assume hIncreasing hChainIdeals.
claim hStationary : stationary_sequence_of_sets K A.
exact (h_s31_l3_increasing_chain_reduction
A hIncreasing hChainIdeals).
exact (andER
(forall n :e omega, A n c= K)
(exists r :e omega, forall n :e omega,
r c= n -> A n = A r)
hStationary).
//GOD1PRF:947655 Now let I be the union of the $\mathrm{I}_{n}$, which is an ideal ; since K is a principal ideal domain, we have $\mathrm{I}=(x)$ for some $x \in \mathrm{~K}$; since $x$ belongs to the union of the $\mathrm{I}_{n}$, we have $x \in \mathrm{I}_{r}$ for some index $r$; but then it is clear that $\mathrm{I}_{r}$ contains all multiples of $x$, in other words that $\mathrm{I}_{r} \supset \mathrm{I}$, so that when $n \geqslant r$ we have
claim h_s31_l3_union_principal : forall A:set -> set,
increasing_sequence_of_sets K A ->
(forall n :e omega, two_sided_ideal K add mul (A n)) ->
exists x :e K,
module_family_union omega A = principal_ideal K add mul x.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).

exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hRegularModule : left_module K add mul K add mul.
exact (god1_ring_left_regular_module K add mul hRing).
claim hPrincipal : forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a.
exact (andER
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists a :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul a)
hPID).
let A.
assume hIncreasing hChainIdeals.
claim hSubmodules : forall n :e omega,
submodule K add mul K add mul (A n).
exact (fun n hn => god1_left_ideal_is_regular_submodule
K add mul (A n)
(andEL
(left_ideal K add mul (A n))
(right_ideal K add mul (A n))
(hChainIdeals n hn))).
claim hDirected :
(exists n, n :e omega)
/\ forall i j :e omega, exists k :e omega,
A i c= A k /\ A j c= A k.
claim hIndexNonempty : exists n, n :e omega.
exact (ex_intro (fun n => n :e omega) 0
(nat_p_omega 0 nat_0)).
claim hCommonUpper : forall i j :e omega,
exists k :e omega, A i c= A k /\ A j c= A k.
let i.
assume hi.
let j.
assume hj.
exact (orE
(i c= j) (j c= i)
(ordinal_linear i j
(nat_p_ordinal i (omega_nat_p i hi))
(nat_p_ordinal j (omega_nat_p j hj)))
(exists k :e omega, A i c= A k /\ A j c= A k)

(fun k => k :e omega /\ (A i c= A k /\ A j c= A k))

(j :e omega)

(A i c= A j) (A j c= A j)

(fun k => k :e omega /\ (A i c= A k /\ A j c= A k))

(andI
(i :e omega)
(A i c= A i /\ A j c= A i)
hi
(andI
(A i c= A i) (A j c= A i)

exact (andI
(exists n, n :e omega)

//GOD1PRF:948180 hence $\mathbf{I}_{\boldsymbol{n}}=\mathbf{I}_{\boldsymbol{r}}$, which proves Lemma 3.
claim h_s31_l3_conclusion :
exists I :e X, forall J :e X, I c= J -> J = I.

//GOD1:948807 maximal_proper_ideal : "#4 is a maximal proper ideal of #1" | $#4\text{ is maximal}$
Definition maximal_proper_ideal :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul I =>
two_sided_ideal K add mul I
/\ I <> K
/\ forall J, two_sided_ideal K add mul J ->
I c= J -> J = I \/ J = K.

Theorem god1_equal_nonzero_principal_ideals_give_unit_multiple :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul -> forall p d :e K,
p <> ring_zero K add ->
principal_ideal K add mul d = principal_ideal K add mul p ->
exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let p.
assume hp.
let d.
assume hd hpNonzero hIdealsEq.
claim hdInD : d :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_contains_generator K add mul hRing d hd).
claim hdInP : d :e principal_ideal K add mul p.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul p) d hIdealsEq hdInD).
claim hpInP : p :e principal_ideal K add mul p.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_contains_generator K add mul hRing p hp).
claim hpInD : p :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
(principal_ideal K add mul d) p
(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul p) hIdealsEq)
hpInP).
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun u:set => mul u p) d hdInP
(exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)).
let u.
assume hu hdEq.
apply (ReplE_impred K (fun v:set => mul v d) p hpInD
(exists q :e K, ring_unit K add mul q /\ d = mul q p)).
let v.
assume hv hpEq.
claim hVU : mul v u :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing v hv u hu).
claim hpFactorEq : p = mul p (mul v u).
exact (eq_i_tra p (mul v d) (mul p (mul v u))
hpEq
(eq_i_tra
(mul v d) (mul v (mul u p)) (mul p (mul v u))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul v z) d (mul u p) hdEq)
(eq_i_tra
(mul v (mul u p)) (mul (mul v u) p)
(mul p (mul v u))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
v hv u hu p hp)
(hComm (mul v u) hVU p hp)))).
claim hIdentityData : ring_one K mul :e K
/\ forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification
K add mul hRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
hIdentityData).
claim hpOne : mul p (ring_one K mul) = p.
exact (andEL
(mul p (ring_one K mul) = p)
(mul (ring_one K mul) p = p)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
hIdentityData) p hp)).
claim hCancelEq : mul p (ring_one K mul) = mul p (mul v u).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul p (ring_one K mul)) p (mul p (mul v u))
hpOne hpFactorEq).
claim hOneEqVU : ring_one K mul = mul v u.
exact (god1_integral_domain_left_cancel K add mul hIntegral
p hp hpNonzero (ring_one K mul) hOne (mul v u) hVU hCancelEq).
claim hVUOne : mul v u = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_sym (ring_one K mul) (mul v u) hOneEqVU).
claim hUVOne : mul u v = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra (mul u v) (mul v u) (ring_one K mul)
(hComm u hu v hv) hVUOne).
claim hUnitU : ring_unit K add mul u.
exact (andI
(u :e K)
(exists w :e K,
mul w u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u w = ring_one K mul)
hu
(ex_intro
(fun w => w :e K
/\ (mul w u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u w = ring_one K mul))
v
(andI
(v :e K)
(mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hv
(andI
(mul v u = ring_one K mul)
(mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hVUOne hUVOne)))).
exact (ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ (ring_unit K add mul q /\ d = mul q p))
u
(andI
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hu
(andI
(ring_unit K add mul u) (d = mul u p)
hUnitU hdEq))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_divisor_condition_iff_maximal_principal_ideal :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall p :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
p <> ring_zero K add -> not (ring_unit K add mul p) ->
((forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
<-> maximal_proper_ideal K add mul
(principal_ideal K add mul p)).
let K add mul p.
assume hp hPID hpNonzero hNonunitP.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
claim hPrincipalP : two_sided_ideal K add mul
(principal_ideal K add mul p).
exact (god1_principal_ideal_is_ideal K add mul p hp hCommRing).
claim hPrincipalPSubset : principal_ideal K add mul p c= K.
exact (god1_subgroup_subset K add
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
(god1_principal_ideal_additive_subgroup K add mul p hp hRing)).
apply iffI.
- assume hDivisorCondition.
claim hProper : principal_ideal K add mul p <> K.
assume hPrincipalWhole.

exact (mem_eq_set_subst K (principal_ideal K add mul p)
(ring_one K mul)
(eq_sym (principal_ideal K add mul p) K hPrincipalWhole)
hOne).

(ring_divides K mul p (ring_one K mul))
(ring_one K mul :e principal_ideal K add mul p)

hOneInP).
exact (hNonunitP
(iffER
(ring_unit K add mul p)
(ring_divides K mul p (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one
K add mul hCommRing p hp)
hPDividesOne)).
claim hMaximal : forall J,
two_sided_ideal K add mul J ->
principal_ideal K add mul p c= J ->
J = principal_ideal K add mul p \/ J = K.
let J.
assume hJ hPSubJ.

let d.

\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.

(ring_unit K add mul d)
(exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hChoices
(J = principal_ideal K add mul p \/ J = K)).

(J = principal_ideal K add mul p) (J = K)

hJEq
(god1_principal_ideal_of_unit_is_whole_ring
K add mul hRing d hUnitD))).
assume hAssociateExists.
apply hAssociateExists.
let u.
assume huData.
claim hu : u :e K.
exact (andEL
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p) huData).
claim hAssociateData : ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p) huData).
claim hUnitU : ring_unit K add mul u.
exact (andEL
(ring_unit K add mul u) (d = mul u p) hAssociateData).
claim hdEq : d = mul u p.
exact (andER
(ring_unit K add mul u) (d = mul u p) hAssociateData).
claim hPrincipalDEqUP : principal_ideal K add mul d
= principal_ideal K add mul (mul u p).
exact (f_eq_i

d (mul u p) hdEq).

= principal_ideal K add mul p.

K add mul hCommRing u hu p hp hUnitU).
exact (orIL
(J = principal_ideal K add mul p) (J = K)

(principal_ideal K add mul p) hJEq
(eq_i_tra
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u p))
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
hPrincipalDEqUP hPrincipalUP))).
exact (andI
(two_sided_ideal K add mul (principal_ideal K add mul p)
/\ principal_ideal K add mul p <> K)
(forall J, two_sided_ideal K add mul J ->
principal_ideal K add mul p c= J ->
J = principal_ideal K add mul p \/ J = K)
(andI
(two_sided_ideal K add mul (principal_ideal K add mul p))
(principal_ideal K add mul p <> K)
hPrincipalP hProper)
hMaximal).
- assume hMaximalIdeal.

assume hd hDDividesP.

(principal_ideal K add mul d).

exact (god1_subgroup_subset K add
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_principal_ideal_additive_subgroup K add mul d hd hRing)).
claim hPSubD : principal_ideal K add mul p
c= principal_ideal K add mul d.

assume hzP.

(ring_divides K mul p z)

(ring_divides K mul d z)

(ring_unit K add mul d

(ring_unit K add mul d)

(god1_equal_nonzero_principal_ideals_give_unit_multiple

assume hPrincipalWhole.
claim hOneInD : ring_one K mul :e principal_ideal K add mul d.

(ring_one K mul)
(eq_sym (principal_ideal K add mul d) K hPrincipalWhole)
hOne).
claim hDDividesOne : ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul).

(ring_divides K mul d (ring_one K mul))

Theorem god1_extremal_coprime_or_divides :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
ring_divides K mul p x \/ coprime_elements K add mul p x.
let K add mul p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx hPID hExtremal.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hExtremalDivisors : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
exact (andER
(((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p)))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hExtremal).
apply (orE
(ring_divides K mul p x)
(not (ring_divides K mul p x))
(xm (ring_divides K mul p x))
(ring_divides K mul p x \/ coprime_elements K add mul p x)).
assume hPDividesX.
exact (orIL
(ring_divides K mul p x)
(coprime_elements K add mul p x) hPDividesX).
assume hPNotDividesX.
apply (orIR
(ring_divides K mul p x)
(coprime_elements K add mul p x)).
apply (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul p x)
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p /\ ring_divides K mul d x ->
ring_unit K add mul d)
(god1_coprime_elements_common_divisor_characterization
K add mul p hp x hx hPID)).
let d.
assume hd hCommon.
claim hDDividesP : ring_divides K mul d p.
exact (andEL
(ring_divides K mul d p)
(ring_divides K mul d x) hCommon).
claim hDDividesX : ring_divides K mul d x.
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul d p)
(ring_divides K mul d x) hCommon).
claim hChoices : ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
exact (hExtremalDivisors d hd hDDividesP).
apply (orE
(ring_unit K add mul d)
(exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hChoices (ring_unit K add mul d)).
assume hUnitD.
exact hUnitD.
assume hAssociateExists.
apply hAssociateExists.
let u.
assume huData.
claim hu : u :e K.
exact (andEL
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p) huData).
claim hAssociateData : ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p) huData).
claim hdEq : d = mul u p.
exact (andER
(ring_unit K add mul u) (d = mul u p) hAssociateData).
claim hPDividesD : ring_divides K mul p d.
exact (andI
(p :e K /\ d :e K)
(exists q :e K, d = mul q p)
(andI (p :e K) (d :e K) hp hd)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ d = mul q p)
u (andI (u :e K) (d = mul u p) hu hdEq))).
claim hPDividesX : ring_divides K mul p x.
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
p hp d hd x hx hPDividesD hDDividesX).
exact (FalseE (hPNotDividesX hPDividesX)
(ring_unit K add mul d)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_element_divides_zero :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d (ring_zero K add).
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
claim hZero : ring_zero K add :e K.
exact (god1_group_identity_in K add
(god1_ring_additive_group K add mul hRing)).
let d.
assume hd.
claim hZeroProduct : mul (ring_zero K add) d = ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_ring_zero_multiplication_left
K add mul hRing d hd).
exact (andI
(d :e K /\ ring_zero K add :e K)
(exists q :e K, ring_zero K add = mul q d)
(andI
(d :e K) (ring_zero K add :e K) hd hZero)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ ring_zero K add = mul q d)
(ring_zero K add)
(andI
(ring_zero K add :e K)
(ring_zero K add = mul (ring_zero K add) d)
hZero
(eq_sym
(mul (ring_zero K add) d)
(ring_zero K add) hZeroProduct)))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_divides_binary_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
ring_divides K mul p (mul x y) ->
ring_divides K mul p x \/ ring_divides K mul p y.
let K add mul p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hExtremal hPDividesProduct.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
apply (orE
(x = ring_zero K add)
(x <> ring_zero K add)
(xm (x = ring_zero K add))
(ring_divides K mul p x \/ ring_divides K mul p y)).
assume hxZero.
exact (orIL
(ring_divides K mul p x) (ring_divides K mul p y)
(god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul p z)
(ring_zero K add) x
(eq_sym x (ring_zero K add) hxZero)
(god1_ring_element_divides_zero K add mul hRing p hp))).
assume hxNonzero.
apply (orE
(y = ring_zero K add)
(y <> ring_zero K add)
(xm (y = ring_zero K add))
(ring_divides K mul p x \/ ring_divides K mul p y)).
assume hyZero.
exact (orIR
(ring_divides K mul p x) (ring_divides K mul p y)
(god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul p z)
(ring_zero K add) y
(eq_sym y (ring_zero K add) hyZero)
(god1_ring_element_divides_zero K add mul hRing p hp))).
assume hyNonzero.
claim hCases : ring_divides K mul p x
\/ coprime_elements K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_coprime_or_divides
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hExtremal).
apply (orE
(ring_divides K mul p x)
(coprime_elements K add mul p x)
hCases
(ring_divides K mul p x \/ ring_divides K mul p y)).
assume hPDividesX.
exact (orIL
(ring_divides K mul p x) (ring_divides K mul p y)
hPDividesX).
assume hCoprimePX.
exact (orIR
(ring_divides K mul p x) (ring_divides K mul p y)
(god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma
K add mul x hx y hy p hp hPID
hxNonzero hyNonzero hPDividesProduct hCoprimePX)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_divides_finite_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul n f) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (f i).
let K add mul p.
assume hp hPID hExtremal.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hNonunitP : not (ring_unit K add mul p).
exact (andER
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(andEL
((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hExtremal)).
claim hBase : forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e 0, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f) ->
exists i :e 0, ring_divides K mul p (f i).
let f.
assume hMaps hDividesEmpty.
claim hEmptyProduct : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul f).
claim hPDividesOne : ring_divides K mul p (ring_one K mul).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul p z)
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f)
(ring_one K mul) hEmptyProduct hDividesEmpty).
claim hUnitP : ring_unit K add mul p.
exact (iffER
(ring_unit K add mul p)
(ring_divides K mul p (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one
K add mul hCommRing p hp)
hPDividesOne).
exact (FalseE (hNonunitP hUnitP)
(exists i :e 0, ring_divides K mul p (f i))).
claim hStep : forall m, nat_p m ->
(forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e m, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) ->
exists i :e m, ring_divides K mul p (f i)) ->
forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f) ->
exists i :e ordsucc m, ring_divides K mul p (f i).
let m.
assume hm hInduction.
let f.
assume hMaps hDividesSuccessor.
claim hmOmega : m :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega m hm).
claim hPrefixMaps : forall i :e m, f i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => hMaps i (ordsuccI1 m i hi)).
claim hPrefixIn : ring_finite_product K add mul m f :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing m
(nat_finite m hm) f hPrefixMaps).
claim hLastIn : f m :e K.
exact (hMaps m (ordsuccI2 m)).
claim hSuccessorProduct :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m).
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_natural_successor
K add mul m hmOmega f).
claim hDividesBinary : ring_divides K mul p
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m)).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul p z)
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
hSuccessorProduct hDividesSuccessor).
claim hCases :
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul m f)
\/ ring_divides K mul p (f m).
exact (god1_extremal_divides_binary_product
K add mul p hp
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f) hPrefixIn
(f m) hLastIn hPID hExtremal hDividesBinary).
apply (orE
(ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul m f))
(ring_divides K mul p (f m)) hCases
(exists i :e ordsucc m, ring_divides K mul p (f i))).
assume hDividesPrefix.
claim hPrefixWitness : exists i :e m,
ring_divides K mul p (f i).
exact (hInduction f hPrefixMaps hDividesPrefix).
apply hPrefixWitness.
let i.
assume hiData.
claim hi : i :e m.
exact (andEL
(i :e m) (ring_divides K mul p (f i)) hiData).
claim hDividesI : ring_divides K mul p (f i).
exact (andER
(i :e m) (ring_divides K mul p (f i)) hiData).
exact (ex_intro
(fun j => j :e ordsucc m /\ ring_divides K mul p (f j))
i
(andI
(i :e ordsucc m) (ring_divides K mul p (f i))
(ordsuccI1 m i hi) hDividesI)).
assume hDividesLast.
exact (ex_intro
(fun i => i :e ordsucc m /\ ring_divides K mul p (f i))
m
(andI
(m :e ordsucc m) (ring_divides K mul p (f m))
(ordsuccI2 m) hDividesLast)).
claim hAll : forall q, nat_p q -> forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul q f) ->
exists i :e q, ring_divides K mul p (f i).
exact (nat_ind
(fun q => forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e q, f i :e K) ->
ring_divides K mul p (ring_finite_product K add mul q f) ->
exists i :e q, ring_divides K mul p (f i))
hBase hStep).
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
assume hMaps hDividesProduct.
exact (hAll n (omega_nat_p n hn) f hMaps hDividesProduct).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_unit_multiple :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
forall q u p :e K,
extremal_element K add mul q ->
ring_unit K add mul u ->
p = mul u q -> extremal_element K add mul p.
let K add mul.
assume hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hOneNonzero : ring_one K mul <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_one_ne_zero K add mul hIntegral).
claim hOne : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
let q.
assume hq.
let u.
assume hu.
let p.
assume hp hExtremalQ hUnitU hpEq.
claim hQPrefix :
(q :e K /\ q <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul q).
exact (andEL
((q :e K /\ q <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul q))
(forall d :e K,

Theorem god1_s31_theorem6_prime_divisor_interface :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall p :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
p <> ring_zero K add -> not (ring_unit K add mul p) ->
(extremal_element K add mul p
<-> forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i)).
let K add mul p.
assume hp hPID hpNonzero hNonunitP.
apply iffI.
- assume hExtremal.
let n.
assume hn.
let x.
assume hx hDividesProduct.
claim hMaps : forall i :e n, x i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => ap_Pi n (fun j => K) x i hx hi).
exact (god1_extremal_divides_finite_product
K add mul p hp hPID hExtremal n hn
(fun i => x i) hMaps hDividesProduct).
- assume hPrimeProduct.
exact (god1_finite_product_prime_property_implies_extremal
K add mul p hp hPID hpNonzero hNonunitP hPrimeProduct).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_theorem6_extremal_characterizations :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall p :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
p <> ring_zero K add -> not (ring_unit K add mul p) ->
(extremal_element K add mul p
<-> forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
/\ ((forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
<-> maximal_proper_ideal K add mul (principal_ideal K add mul p))
/\ (maximal_proper_ideal K add mul (principal_ideal K add mul p)
<-> forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i)).
let K add mul p.
assume hp hPID hpne hNonunit.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
//GOD1PRF:948487 theorem 6. Let $p$ be an element of a principal ideal domain K , and suppose that $p$ is neither zero nor a anit. Then the following properties are equivalent:\\
claim h_s31_t6_statement :
extremal_element K add mul p
<-> forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i).
exact (god1_s31_theorem6_prime_divisor_interface
K add mul p hp hPID hpne hNonunit).
//GOD1PRF:949002 The equivalence of $a$ ) and $b$ ) is just the definition of extremal elements. To show that $b$ ) and $c$ ) are equivalent, consider an ideal J containing I ; since K is a principal ideal domain we have $\mathrm{J}=(x)$ for some $x \in \mathrm{~K}$, and to say that J contains I means that $x$ divides $p$; moreover, the relation $\mathrm{J}=\mathrm{K}$ means that $x$ is a unit of K , and the relation $\mathrm{J}=\mathrm{I}$ means that $x=p u$, where $u$ is a unit. The equivalence of $b$ ) and $c$ ) is clear from these remarks.
claim h_s31_t6_extremal_maximal_equivalence :
(forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
<-> maximal_proper_ideal K add mul (principal_ideal K add mul p).
exact (god1_extremal_divisor_condition_iff_maximal_principal_ideal
K add mul p hp hPID hpne hNonunit).
//GOD1PRF:949536 Finally, let us show that the property $d$ ) also characterizes extremal elements. Suppose that $p$ is extremal, and let $x_{1}, \ldots, x_{n}$ be non-zero elements of K such that $p$ divides the product $x_{1} \ldots x_{n}$. To show that $p$ divides at least one of the $x_{i}$, write
claim h_s31_t6_extremal_implies_prime_product : extremal_element K add mul p ->
forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i).
exact (iffEL
(extremal_element K add mul p)
(forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i))
h_s31_t6_statement).
//GOD1PRF:949889 an obvious inductive argument then shows that it is sufficient to examine the case $n=2$, in other words to prove that if $p$ divides $x y$, then either $p$ divides $x$ or $p$ divides $y$. By Theorem 2 this reduces to proving that, for all $x \neq 0$ in K, either $p$ divides $x$ or else $p$ and $x$ are coprime. Consider the ideal $(p, x)$ generated by $p$ and $x$; clearly this ideal contains the ideal ( $p$ ), and by condition $c$ ) of Theorem 6, which has already been proved, there are exactly two possibilities : either
claim h_s31_t6_theorem2_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 y0 d0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> y0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 (mul0 x0 y0) ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 d0 x0 ->
ring_divides K0 mul0 d0 y0.
apply god1_s31_theorem2_euclid_coprime_divisor_lemma.
claim h_s31_t6_self_condition_c_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall p0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
p0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> not (ring_unit K0 add0 mul0 p0) ->
(extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 p0
<-> forall n0 :e omega, forall x0 :e K0 :^: n0,
ring_divides K0 mul0 p0
(ring_finite_product K0 add0 mul0 n0 (fun i => x0 i)) ->
exists i :e n0, ring_divides K0 mul0 p0 (x0 i)).
apply god1_s31_theorem6_prime_divisor_interface.
//GOD1PRF:950506 in which case $x$ belongs to $(p)$ and is therefore a multiple of $p$.\\
claim h_s31_t6_divisibility_case : forall x :e K,
x :e principal_ideal K add mul p -> ring_divides K mul p x.
let x.
assume hx hPrincipal.
exact (iffER
(ring_divides K mul p x)
(x :e principal_ideal K add mul p)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing p hp x hx)
hPrincipal).
//GOD1PRF:950579 We have therefore shown that every extremal element of K satisfies $d$ ). Conversely, let $p$ be an element of K which is neither zero nor a unit, and which satisfies $d$ ). By Theorem 5, $p$ can be written in the form
claim h_s31_t6_theorem5_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall x0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> factorization_into_extremals K0 add0 mul0 x0.
apply god1_s31_theorem5_existence_of_extremal_factorization.
claim h_s31_t6_factorization_of_p : factorization_into_extremals K add mul p.
exact (god1_s31_theorem5_existence_of_extremal_factorization
K add mul p hp hPID hpne).
//GOD1PRF:950827 where the $p_{i}$ are extremal. By $\left.d\right), p$ divides at least one of the $p_{i}$; but since $p_{i}$ is extremal and $p$ is not a unit, it follows that $p=u p_{i}$ where $u$ is a unit, and hence $p$ is extremal. This completes the proof.
claim h_s31_t6_conclusion :
extremal_element K add mul p
<-> forall n :e omega, forall x :e K :^: n,
ring_divides K mul p
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => x i)) ->
exists i :e n, ring_divides K mul p (x i).
exact h_s31_t6_statement.

claim hExtremalDivisorEquivalence :
extremal_element K add mul p
<-> forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p.
exact (iffI
(extremal_element K add mul p)
(forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
(fun hExtremal => andER
(((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p)))
(forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hExtremal)
(fun hDivisorCondition => andI
((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(forall d :e K, ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
(andI
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(andI
(p :e K) (p <> ring_zero K add) hp hpne)

Theorem god1_s31_theorem6_corollary_coprime_to_each_factor :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall x :e K, forall y :e K :^: n,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> (forall i :e n, y i <> ring_zero K add) ->
(forall i :e n, coprime_elements K add mul x (y i)) ->
coprime_elements K add mul x
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => y i)).
let K add mul.
let n.
assume hn.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hxne hYne hCoprime.
//GOD1PRF:951075 COROLLARY. Let $x, y_{1}, \ldots, y_{n}$ be non-zero elements of a principal ideal domain K , and suppose that $x$ and $y_{i}$ are coprime for $i=1, \ldots, n$. Then $x$ is prime to the product $y_{1} \ldots y_{n}$.
claim h_s31_t6c_statement :
coprime_elements K add mul x
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => y i)).
claim hMaps : forall i :e n, y i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => ap_Pi n (fun j => K) y i hy hi).
exact (god1_coprime_elements_finite_product
K add mul hPID x hx n hn (fun i => y i)
hMaps hYne hCoprime).
//GOD1PRF:951292 Suppose that $x$ and $y_{1}, \ldots, y_{n}$ have a common divisor $d$ which is not a unit; then $d$ is a product of extremal elements and is therefore a multiple of at least one extremal element. Consequently there exists an extremal element $p$ which divides both $x$ and $y_{1} \ldots y_{n}$. By Theorem 6, $d$ ), there exists an index $i$ such that $p$ divides $y_{i}$, contrary to the hypothesis that $x$ and $y_{i}$ are coprime.
claim h_s31_t6c_theorem6_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall p0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
p0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> not (ring_unit K0 add0 mul0 p0) ->
(extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 p0
<-> forall n0 :e omega, forall x0 :e K0 :^: n0,
ring_divides K0 mul0 p0
(ring_finite_product K0 add0 mul0 n0 (fun i => x0 i)) ->
exists i :e n0, ring_divides K0 mul0 p0 (x0 i)).
apply god1_s31_theorem6_prime_divisor_interface.
claim h_s31_t6c_conclusion :
coprime_elements K add mul x
(ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun i => y i)).
exact h_s31_t6c_statement.
exact h_s31_t6c_conclusion.
Qed.

//GOD1:952017 associated_elements : "#4 and #5 are associated elements of #1" | $#4\sim #5$
Definition associated_elements :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) ->
set -> set -> prop :=
fun K add mul x y =>
x :e K /\ y :e K
/\ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ y = mul u x.

Theorem god1_extremal_divisor_is_associated :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p q :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_element K add mul q ->
ring_divides K mul p q ->
associated_elements K add mul p q.
let K add mul p.
assume hp.
let q.
assume hq hPID hExtremalP hExtremalQ hPDividesQ.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hPNonzeroAndNonunit :
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p).
exact (andEL
((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hExtremalP).
claim hpNonzero : p <> ring_zero K add.
exact (andER
(p :e K) (p <> ring_zero K add)
(andEL
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul p)) hPNonzeroAndNonunit)).
claim hNonunitP : not (ring_unit K add mul p).
exact (andER
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul p)) hPNonzeroAndNonunit).
claim hQDivisorCondition : forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d q ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u q.
exact (andER
(((q :e K /\ q <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul q)))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d q ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u q)
hExtremalQ).
claim hCases : ring_unit K add mul p
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ p = mul u q.
exact (hQDivisorCondition p hp hPDividesQ).
claim hAssociateExists : exists v :e K,
ring_unit K add mul v /\ q = mul v p.
apply (orE
(ring_unit K add mul p)
(exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ p = mul u q)
hCases
(exists v :e K, ring_unit K add mul v /\ q = mul v p)).
assume hUnitP.
exact (FalseE (hNonunitP hUnitP)
(exists v :e K, ring_unit K add mul v /\ q = mul v p)).
assume hUnitMultipleExists.
apply hUnitMultipleExists.
let u.
assume huData.
claim hu : u :e K.
exact (andEL
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ p = mul u q) huData).
claim hUnitMultipleData : ring_unit K add mul u /\ p = mul u q.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(ring_unit K add mul u /\ p = mul u q) huData).
claim hUnitU : ring_unit K add mul u.
exact (andEL
(ring_unit K add mul u) (p = mul u q) hUnitMultipleData).
claim hpEq : p = mul u q.
exact (andER
(ring_unit K add mul u) (p = mul u q) hUnitMultipleData).
claim hPrincipalPEqQ : principal_ideal K add mul p
= principal_ideal K add mul q.
exact (eq_i_tra
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
(principal_ideal K add mul (mul u q))
(principal_ideal K add mul q)
(f_eq_i
(fun z => principal_ideal K add mul z)
p (mul u q) hpEq)
(god1_principal_ideal_unit_multiple
K add mul hCommRing u hu q hq hUnitU)).
exact (god1_equal_nonzero_principal_ideals_give_unit_multiple
K add mul hIntegral p hp q hq hpNonzero
(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul p)
(principal_ideal K add mul q) hPrincipalPEqQ)).
exact (andI
(p :e K /\ q :e K)
(exists v :e K, ring_unit K add mul v /\ q = mul v p)
(andI (p :e K) (q :e K) hp hq)
hAssociateExists).
Qed.

Theorem god1_finite_product_is_divisible_by_each_factor :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul ->
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
forall i :e n,
ring_divides K mul (f i) (ring_finite_product K add mul n f).

claim hBase : forall f:set -> set,

(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 f))).
claim hStep : forall m, nat_p m ->
(forall f:set -> set,

ring_divides K mul (f i) (ring_finite_product K add mul m f)) ->
forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc m, f i :e K) ->
forall i :e ordsucc m,

(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f).

assume hm hInduction.
let f.
assume hMaps.

exact (nat_p_omega m hm).

(nat_finite (ordsucc m) (nat_ordsucc m hm)) f hMaps).
claim hSuccessorProduct :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m).
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_natural_successor
K add mul m hmOmega f).
claim hSuccessorProductComm :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (f m) (ring_finite_product K add mul m f).
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f)

(f m :e K
/\ ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f :e K)

(f m :e K)
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f :e K)
hLastIn hProductIn)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K
/\ ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f = mul q (f m))
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f)
(andI
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f :e K)
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f
= mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m f) (f m))
hPrefixIn hSuccessorProduct))).
let i.
assume hi.
claim hIndexCases : i :e m \/ i = m.
exact (ordsuccE m i hi).
apply (orE
(i :e m) (i = m) hIndexCases
(ring_divides K mul (f i)
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f))).
assume hiPrefix.
claim hFactorDividesPrefix : ring_divides K mul (f i)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f).
exact (hInduction f hPrefixMaps i hiPrefix).
claim hPrefixDividesProduct : ring_divides K mul
(ring_finite_product K add mul m f)
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) f).

(ring_finite_product K add mul m f :e K)

(f i) (hPrefixMaps i hiPrefix)

assume hi.

Theorem god1_extremal_factor_matches_factor_of_equal_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall m n :e omega,
forall p:set -> set, forall q:set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(forall i :e m, p i :e K) ->
(forall j :e n, q j :e K) ->
(forall i :e m, extremal_element K add mul (p i)) ->
(forall j :e n, extremal_element K add mul (q j)) ->
ring_finite_product K add mul m p
= ring_finite_product K add mul n q ->
forall i :e m,
exists j :e n, associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q j).
let K add mul.
let m.
assume hm.
let n.
assume hn.
let p q.
assume hPID hPMaps hQMaps hPExtremal hQExtremal hProductsEq.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
let i.
assume hi.
claim hFactorDividesLeft : ring_divides K mul (p i)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p).
exact (god1_finite_product_is_divisible_by_each_factor
K add mul hCommRing m hm p hPMaps i hi).
claim hFactorDividesRight : ring_divides K mul (p i)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul (p i) z)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q)
hProductsEq hFactorDividesLeft).
claim hDividedFactorExists : exists j :e n,
ring_divides K mul (p i) (q j).
exact (god1_extremal_divides_finite_product
K add mul (p i) (hPMaps i hi)
hPID (hPExtremal i hi) n hn q hQMaps hFactorDividesRight).
apply hDividedFactorExists.
let j.
assume hjData.
claim hj : j :e n.
exact (andEL
(j :e n) (ring_divides K mul (p i) (q j)) hjData).
claim hDivides : ring_divides K mul (p i) (q j).
exact (andER
(j :e n) (ring_divides K mul (p i) (q j)) hjData).
exact (ex_intro
(fun k => k :e n
/\ associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q k))
j
(andI
(j :e n)
(associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q j))
hj
(god1_extremal_divisor_is_associated
K add mul (p i) (hPMaps i hi) (q j) (hQMaps j hj)
hPID (hPExtremal i hi) (hQExtremal j hj) hDivides))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_divides_unit_multiple_iff :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul -> forall d u x :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u ->
(ring_divides K mul d (mul u x) <-> ring_divides K mul d x).
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let d.
assume hd.
let u.
assume hu.
let x.
assume hx hUnitU.
claim hUX : mul u x :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing u hu x hx).
claim hPrincipalD : two_sided_ideal K add mul
(principal_ideal K add mul d).
exact (god1_principal_ideal_is_ideal K add mul d hd hCommRing).
claim hPrincipalAbsorbs : forall a :e K,
forall z :e principal_ideal K add mul d,
mul a z :e principal_ideal K add mul d
/\ mul z a :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_absorbs
K add mul d hd hCommRing).
claim hInverseSpec : reflection K mul (ring_one K mul)
u (ring_inverse K add mul u).
exact (god1_ring_inverse_specification K add mul u hUnitU).
claim hInversePrefix : ring_inverse K add mul u :e K
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul.
exact (andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul)
(mul u (ring_inverse K add mul u) = ring_one K mul)
hInverseSpec).
claim hInv : ring_inverse K add mul u :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul)
hInversePrefix).
claim hInvU : mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul)
hInversePrefix).
claim hOneLeft : mul (ring_one K mul) x = x.
exact (andER
(mul x (ring_one K mul) = x)
(mul (ring_one K mul) x = x)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification
K add mul hRing)) x hx)).
claim hRecoverX : mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) (mul u x) = x.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) (mul u x))
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u) x) x
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul u) hInv u hu x hx)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u) x)
(mul (ring_one K mul) x) x
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul z x)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u)
(ring_one K mul) hInvU)
hOneLeft)).
apply iffI.
- assume hDividesUX.
claim hUXInPrincipal : mul u x :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(ring_divides K mul d (mul u x))
(mul u x :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd (mul u x) hUX)
hDividesUX).
claim hRecoveredInPrincipal :
mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) (mul u x)
:e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (andEL
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) (mul u x)
:e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(mul (mul u x) (ring_inverse K add mul u)
:e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(hPrincipalAbsorbs
(ring_inverse K add mul u) hInv
(mul u x) hUXInPrincipal)).
claim hxInPrincipal : x :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (mem_eq_substR
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) (mul u x)) x
hRecoverX hRecoveredInPrincipal).
exact (iffER
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(x :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd x hx)
hxInPrincipal).
- assume hDividesX.
claim hxInPrincipal : x :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (iffEL
(ring_divides K mul d x)
(x :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd x hx)
hDividesX).
claim hUXInPrincipal : mul u x :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (andEL
(mul u x :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(mul x u :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(hPrincipalAbsorbs u hu x hxInPrincipal)).
exact (iffER
(ring_divides K mul d (mul u x))
(mul u x :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd (mul u x) hUX)
hUXInPrincipal).
Qed.

Theorem god1_swap_finite_family_factor_to_last :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul ->
forall k, nat_p k -> forall j :e ordsucc k,
forall q:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc k, q i :e K) ->
(permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k :e permutation_group (ordsucc k)
/\ ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k) q
= ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k)
(fun i => q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k i)))
/\ q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k k) = q j.
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
let k.
assume hk.
let j.
assume hj.
let q.
assume hMaps.
claim hLast : k :e ordsucc k.
exact (ordsuccI2 k).
claim hSwapIn : permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k
:e permutation_group (ordsucc k).
exact (god1_permutation_swap_in (ordsucc k) j k hj hLast).
claim hProductInvariant :
ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k) q
= ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k)
(fun i => q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k i)).
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_bijection_invariant
K add mul hCommRing
(ordsucc k) (ordsucc k)
(nat_finite (ordsucc k) (nat_ordsucc k hk))
(nat_finite (ordsucc k) (nat_ordsucc k hk))
(fun i => permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k i)
(god1_permutation_swap_bijective (ordsucc k) j k hj hLast)
q hMaps).
claim hLastValue : q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k k) = q j.
exact (f_eq_i q
(permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k k) j
(god1_permutation_swap_at_right (ordsucc k) j k hj hLast)).
exact (andI
(permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k :e permutation_group (ordsucc k)
/\ ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k) q
= ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k)
(fun i => q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k i)))
(q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k k) = q j)
(andI
(permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k
:e permutation_group (ordsucc k))
(ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k) q
= ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc k)
(fun i => q (permutation_swap (ordsucc k) j k i)))
hSwapIn hProductInvariant)
hLastValue).
Qed.

Theorem god1_cancel_associated_last_factors :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul ->
forall P Q p u v :e K,
p <> ring_zero K add ->
mul P p = mul u (mul Q (mul v p)) ->
P = mul (mul u v) Q.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let P.
assume hP.
let Q.
assume hQ.
let p.
assume hp.
let u.
assume hu.
let v.
assume hv hpNonzero hEquation.
claim hUV : mul u v :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing u hu v hv).
claim hUVQ : mul (mul u v) Q :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
(mul u v) hUV Q hQ).
claim hQVP : mul Q (mul v p) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
Q hQ (mul v p)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing v hv p hp)).
claim hReassociate : mul u (mul Q (mul v p))
= mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul u (mul Q (mul v p)))
(mul Q (mul u (mul v p)))
(mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p)
(god1_commutative_ring_three_factor_interchange
K add mul hCommRing u hu Q hQ
(mul v p)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing v hv p hp))
(eq_i_tra
(mul Q (mul u (mul v p)))
(mul Q (mul (mul u v) p))
(mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul Q z)
(mul u (mul v p)) (mul (mul u v) p)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
u hu v hv p hp))
(eq_i_tra
(mul Q (mul (mul u v) p))
(mul (mul Q (mul u v)) p)
(mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
Q hQ (mul u v) hUV p hp)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul z p)
(mul Q (mul u v)) (mul (mul u v) Q)
(hComm Q hQ (mul u v) hUV))))).
claim hCancelEquation : mul P p = mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul P p) (mul u (mul Q (mul v p)))
(mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p)
hEquation hReassociate).
claim hCancelEquationLeft : mul p P = mul p (mul (mul u v) Q).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul p P) (mul P p) (mul p (mul (mul u v) Q))
(hComm p hp P hP)
(eq_i_tra
(mul P p) (mul (mul (mul u v) Q) p)
(mul p (mul (mul u v) Q))
hCancelEquation
(hComm (mul (mul u v) Q) hUVQ p hp))).
exact (god1_integral_domain_left_cancel K add mul hIntegral
p hp hpNonzero P hP (mul (mul u v) Q) hUVQ
hCancelEquationLeft).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_finite_product_unit_implies_empty :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e n, f i :e K) ->
(forall i :e n, extremal_element K add mul (f i)) ->
ring_unit K add mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n f) ->
n = 0.
let K add mul.
assume hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
assume hMaps hExtremal hProductUnit.
apply (orE
(n = 0) (n <> 0) (xm (n = 0)) (n = 0)).
assume hnZero.
exact hnZero.
assume hnNonzero.
claim hZeroN : 0 :e n.
exact (god1_natural_nonzero_contains_zero n hn hnNonzero).
claim hFactorExtremal : extremal_element K add mul (f 0).
exact (hExtremal 0 hZeroN).
claim hFactorNonunit : not (ring_unit K add mul (f 0)).
exact (andER
(f 0 :e K /\ f 0 <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul (f 0)))
(andEL
((f 0 :e K /\ f 0 <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul (f 0)))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d (f 0) ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u (f 0))
hFactorExtremal)).
claim hProductIn : ring_finite_product K add mul n f :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing n
(nat_finite n (omega_nat_p n hn)) f hMaps).
claim hFactorDividesProduct : ring_divides K mul (f 0)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f).
exact (god1_finite_product_is_divisible_by_each_factor
K add mul hCommRing n hn f hMaps 0 hZeroN).
claim hProductDividesOne : ring_divides K mul
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f) (ring_one K mul).
exact (iffEL
(ring_unit K add mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n f))
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f) (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one K add mul hCommRing
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f) hProductIn)
hProductUnit).
claim hFactorDividesOne : ring_divides K mul (f 0) (ring_one K mul).
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
(f 0) (hMaps 0 hZeroN)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n f) hProductIn
(ring_one K mul)
(andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
hFactorDividesProduct hProductDividesOne).
claim hFactorUnit : ring_unit K add mul (f 0).
exact (iffER
(ring_unit K add mul (f 0))
(ring_divides K mul (f 0) (ring_one K mul))
(god1_ring_unit_iff_divides_one
K add mul hCommRing (f 0) (hMaps 0 hZeroN))
hFactorDividesOne).
exact (FalseE (hFactorNonunit hFactorUnit) (n = 0)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_factorization_uniqueness_up_to_unit_core :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
forall m :e omega, forall n :e omega,
forall p q:set -> set,
(forall i :e m, p i :e K) ->
(forall j :e n, q j :e K) ->
(forall i :e m, extremal_element K add mul (p i)) ->
(forall j :e n, extremal_element K add mul (q j)) ->
forall u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u ->
ring_finite_product K add mul m p
= mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) ->
m = n
/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)).
let K add mul.
assume hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).

exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hBase : forall n :e omega,
forall p q:set -> set,
(forall i :e 0, p i :e K) ->
(forall j :e n, q j :e K) ->
(forall i :e 0, extremal_element K add mul (p i)) ->
(forall j :e n, extremal_element K add mul (q j)) ->
forall u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u ->
ring_finite_product K add mul 0 p
= mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) ->
0 = n
/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)).
let n.
assume hn.
let p q.
assume hPMaps hQMaps hPExtremal hQExtremal.
let u.
assume hu hUnitU hEquation.
claim hQProductIn : ring_finite_product K add mul n q :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing n
(nat_finite n (omega_nat_p n hn)) q hQMaps).
claim hEmptyProduct : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 p
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul p).
claim hOneEqUQ : ring_one K mul
= mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q).
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_one K mul) (ring_finite_product K add mul 0 p)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q))
(eq_sym
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 p)
(ring_one K mul) hEmptyProduct)
hEquation).
claim hUQOne : mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q)
= ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_sym
(ring_one K mul)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q)) hOneEqUQ).
claim hQUOne : mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) u
= ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) u)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q))
(ring_one K mul)
(hComm (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) hQProductIn u hu)
hUQOne).
claim hQProductUnit : ring_unit K add mul
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q).
exact (andI
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q :e K)
(exists v :e K,
mul v (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) = ring_one K mul
/\ mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) v = ring_one K mul)
hQProductIn
(ex_intro
(fun v => v :e K
/\ (mul v (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) = ring_one K mul
/\ mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) v = ring_one K mul))
u
(andI
(u :e K)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) = ring_one K mul
/\ mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) u = ring_one K mul)
hu
(andI
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) = ring_one K mul)
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) u = ring_one K mul)
hUQOne hQUOne)))).
claim hnZero : n = 0.
exact (god1_extremal_finite_product_unit_implies_empty
K add mul hPID n hn q hQMaps hQExtremal hQProductUnit).
claim hAllAssociated : forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul
(p i) (q (permutation_identity n i)).
let i.
assume hi.
exact (FalseE
(EmptyE i (mem_eq_set_subst n 0 i hnZero hi))
(associated_elements K add mul
(p i) (q (permutation_identity n i)))).
exact (andI
(0 = n)
(exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)))
(eq_sym n 0 hnZero)
(ex_intro
(fun sigma => sigma :e permutation_group n
/\ forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)))
(permutation_identity n)
(andI
(permutation_identity n :e permutation_group n)
(forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul
(p i) (q (permutation_identity n i)))
(god1_permutation_identity_in n) hAllAssociated))).
claim hStep : forall a, nat_p a ->
(forall n :e omega,
forall p q:set -> set,
(forall i :e a, p i :e K) ->
(forall j :e n, q j :e K) ->

= mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) ->

/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,

associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i))) ->
forall n :e omega,

/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)).
let a.
assume ha hInduction.

nat_p b /\ n = ordsucc b.

exact (nat_inv n (omega_nat_p n hn)).

(n = 0) (exists b, nat_p b /\ n = ordsucc b)

Theorem god1_s31_theorem7_uniqueness_of_extremal_factorization :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x :e K, forall m n :e omega,
forall p :e K :^: m, forall q :e K :^: n,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> not (ring_unit K add mul x) ->
(forall i :e m, extremal_element K add mul (p i)) ->
(forall j :e n, extremal_element K add mul (q j)) ->
x = ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => p i) ->
x = ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun j => q j) ->
m = n
/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n, associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let m.
assume hm.
let n.
assume hn.
let p.
assume hp.
let q.
assume hq hPID hxne hNonunit hP hQ hProductP hProductQ.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hOneUnit : ring_unit K add mul (ring_one K mul).
exact (god1_ring_one_is_unit K add mul hRing).
claim hPMaps : forall i :e m, p i :e K.
exact (fun i hi => ap_Pi m (fun j => K) p i hp hi).
claim hQMaps : forall j :e n, q j :e K.
exact (fun j hj => ap_Pi n (fun i => K) q j hq hj).
claim hMNonzero : m <> 0.
assume hmZero.
claim hProductIndexEq :
ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => p i)
= ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => p i).
exact (f_eq_i
(fun r => ring_finite_product K add mul r (fun i => p i))
m 0 hmZero).
claim hProductEmpty : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => p i)
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul (fun i => p i)).
claim hxOne : x = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra x
(ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => p i))
(ring_one K mul) hProductP
(eq_i_tra
(ring_finite_product K add mul m (fun i => p i))
(ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => p i))
(ring_one K mul) hProductIndexEq hProductEmpty)).
claim hUnitX : ring_unit K add mul x.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_unit K add mul z)
(ring_one K mul) x
(eq_sym x (ring_one K mul) hxOne) hOneUnit).
exact (hNonunit hUnitX).
claim hNNonzero : n <> 0.
assume hnZero.
claim hProductIndexEq :
ring_finite_product K add mul n (fun j => q j)
= ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun j => q j).
exact (f_eq_i
(fun r => ring_finite_product K add mul r (fun j => q j))

claim hProductEmpty : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun j => q j)
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul (fun j => q j)).
claim hxOne : x = ring_one K mul.
exact (eq_i_tra x

(ring_one K mul) hProductQ

claim hUnitX : ring_unit K add mul x.

Theorem god1_unit_extremal_factorization_lengths_equal :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
forall m n :e omega, forall u v :e K,
forall p q:set -> set,
(forall i :e m, p i :e K) ->
(forall j :e n, q j :e K) ->
(forall i :e m, extremal_element K add mul (p i)) ->
(forall j :e n, extremal_element K add mul (q j)) ->
ring_unit K add mul u -> ring_unit K add mul v ->
mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
= mul v (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) ->
m = n.
let K add mul.
assume hPID.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let m.
assume hm.
let n.
assume hn.
let u.
assume hu.
let v.
assume hv.
let p q.
assume hPMaps hQMaps hPExtremal hQExtremal hUnitU hUnitV hEquation.
claim hPProductIn : ring_finite_product K add mul m p :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing m
(nat_finite m (omega_nat_p m hm)) p hPMaps).
claim hQProductIn : ring_finite_product K add mul n q :e K.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_in K add mul hRing n
(nat_finite n (omega_nat_p n hn)) q hQMaps).
claim hInverseUnit : ring_unit K add mul (ring_inverse K add mul u).
exact (god1_ring_inverse_is_unit K add mul hRing u hUnitU).
claim hInverseIn : ring_inverse K add mul u :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K)
(exists z :e K,
mul z (ring_inverse K add mul u) = ring_one K mul
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) z = ring_one K mul)
hInverseUnit).
claim hInverseTimesU :
mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul)
(andEL
(ring_inverse K add mul u :e K
/\ mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u = ring_one K mul)
(mul u (ring_inverse K add mul u) = ring_one K mul)
(god1_ring_inverse_specification K add mul u hUnitU))).
claim hLeftIdentityP :
mul (ring_one K mul) (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
= ring_finite_product K add mul m p.
exact (andER
(mul (ring_finite_product K add mul m p) (ring_one K mul)
= ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
(mul (ring_one K mul) (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
= ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification
K add mul hRing))
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p) hPProductIn)).
claim hRecoverP :
mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
= ring_finite_product K add mul m p.
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)))
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul u) hInverseIn
u hu (ring_finite_product K add mul m p) hPProductIn)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u)
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
(mul (ring_one K mul) (ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
(f_eq_i
(fun z => mul z (ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) u) (ring_one K mul)
hInverseTimesU)
hLeftIdentityP)).
claim hUnitRatio : ring_unit K add mul
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) v).
exact (god1_ring_unit_product K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul u) v hInverseUnit hUnitV).
claim hRatioIn : mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) v :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul u) hInverseIn v hv).
claim hProductRelation : ring_finite_product K add mul m p
= mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) v)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q).
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p)
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)

(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)))
(ring_finite_product K add mul m p) hRecoverP)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p)))
(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u)
(mul v (ring_finite_product K add mul n q)))
(mul (mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) v)
(ring_finite_product K add mul n q))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) z)
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul m p))
(mul v (ring_finite_product K add mul n q)) hEquation)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
(ring_inverse K add mul u) hInverseIn
v hv (ring_finite_product K add mul n q) hQProductIn))).
claim hCoreResult : m = n
/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)).
exact (god1_extremal_factorization_uniqueness_up_to_unit_core

(mul (ring_inverse K add mul u) v) hRatioIn
hUnitRatio hProductRelation).
exact (andEL
(m = n)
(exists sigma :e permutation_group n,
forall i :e n,
associated_elements K add mul (p i) (q (sigma i)))
hCoreResult).
Qed.

Theorem god1_natural_subset_implies_member_successor :
forall r m, nat_p r -> nat_p m -> r c= m -> r :e ordsucc m.
let r m.
assume hr hm hSub.
claim hCases : (r :e m \/ r = m) \/ m :e r.
exact (ordinal_trichotomy_or r m
(nat_p_ordinal r hr) (nat_p_ordinal m hm)).
exact (orE
(r :e m \/ r = m) (m :e r) hCases
(r :e ordsucc m)
(fun hFirst => orE
(r :e m) (r = m) hFirst
(r :e ordsucc m)
(fun hRM => ordsuccI1 m r hRM)
(fun hEq => mem_eq_substL (ordsucc m) m r
hEq (ordsuccI2 m)))
(fun hMR => FalseE
((nat_not_in_self m hm) (hSub m hMR))
(r :e ordsucc m))).
Qed.

//GOD1:955945 extremal_valuation : "the exponent of extremal element #4 in nonzero element #5" | $v_{#4}(#5)$
Definition extremal_valuation :
set -> (set -> set -> set) -> (set -> set -> set) ->
set -> set -> set :=
fun K add mul p x =>
if x = ring_zero K add
then omega
else Eps_i (fun n => n :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p n) x
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x -> r c= n).

/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x -> r c= n))) x)

r c= Eps_i (fun n =>

(fun n =>

= Eps_i (fun n =>
