Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_monotone_under_divisibility :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
ring_divides K mul x y ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
let K add mul.
let p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero hyNonzero hXDividesY.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hXSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hYSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) y ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp y hy hPID hPExtremal hyNonzero).
claim hXPrefix : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hXSpec).
claim hValXIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hXPrefix).
claim hPowerDividesX : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hXPrefix).
claim hPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValXIn).
claim hPowerDividesY : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) y.
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) hPowerIn
x hx y hy hPowerDividesX hXDividesY).
claim hYMaximal : forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) y ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega

(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) y ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
hYSpec).
exact (hYMaximal
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValXIn hPowerDividesY).
Qed.

Theorem god1_cancel_power_from_divided_product_factor :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul ->
forall p a a1 b :e K, forall r :e omega,
p <> ring_zero K add -> a = mul a1 p ->
ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)) (mul a b) ->
ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a1 b).
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let p.
assume hp.
let a.
assume ha.
let a1.
assume ha1.
let b.
assume hb.
let r.
assume hr hpNonzero hAFactor hPowerDivides.
claim hPowerRIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp r hr).
claim hPowerSuccIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp
(ordsucc r) (omega_ordsucc r hr)).
claim hABIn : mul a b :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing a ha b hb).
claim hA1BIn : mul a1 b :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing a1 ha1 b hb).
claim hQuotientExists : exists c :e K,
mul a b = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)).
exact (andER
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) :e K
/\ mul a b :e K)
(exists c :e K,
mul a b = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))
hPowerDivides).
apply hQuotientExists.
let c.
assume hcData.
claim hc : c :e K.
exact (andEL
(c :e K)
(mul a b = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))
hcData).
claim hProductEquation : mul a b
= mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)).
exact (andER
(c :e K)
(mul a b = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))
hcData).
claim hLeftRearrange : mul a b = mul p (mul a1 b).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul a b) (mul (mul a1 p) b) (mul p (mul a1 b))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul z b) a (mul a1 p) hAFactor)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul a1 p) b) (mul a1 (mul p b))
(mul p (mul a1 b))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative_reverse
K add mul hRing a1 ha1 p hp b hb)
(god1_commutative_ring_triple_swap_first
K add mul hCommRing a1 ha1 p hp b hb))).
claim hPowerSuccessor : ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)
= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_successor K add mul p r
(omega_nat_p r hr)).
claim hRightRearrange :
mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r))
= mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))
(mul c (mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p))
(mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul c z)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p)
hPowerSuccessor)
(eq_i_tra
(mul c (mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p))
(mul c (mul p (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)))
(mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul c z)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p)
(mul p (ring_nat_power K add mul p r))
(hComm (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) hPowerRIn p hp))
(god1_commutative_ring_triple_swap_first
K add mul hCommRing c hc p hp
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) hPowerRIn))).
claim hCommonProduct : mul p (mul a1 b)
= mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul p (mul a1 b)) (mul a b)
(mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)))
(eq_sym (mul a b) (mul p (mul a1 b)) hLeftRearrange)
(eq_i_tra
(mul a b)
(mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))
(mul p (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)))
hProductEquation hRightRearrange)).
claim hCPowerIn :
mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
c hc (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) hPowerRIn).
claim hCancelled : mul a1 b
= mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r).
exact (god1_integral_domain_left_cancel K add mul hIntegral
p hp hpNonzero (mul a1 b) hA1BIn
(mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)) hCPowerIn hCommonProduct).
exact (andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K /\ mul a1 b :e K)
(exists d :e K,
mul a1 b = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p r))
(andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K) (mul a1 b :e K)
hPowerRIn hA1BIn)
(ex_intro
(fun d => d :e K
/\ mul a1 b = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p r))
c
(andI
(c :e K)
(mul a1 b = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r))
hc hCancelled))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_power_successor_divides_after_restoring_factor :

hPowerDivides).

(c :e K)

(c :e K)
(z1 = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p r)) hcData).

= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p.

(c :e K)
(z = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)))

Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_power_divides_product_split :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,

principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
forall r :e omega, forall a b :e K,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a b) ->
exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)

assume hp hPID hPExtremal.

(integral_domain K add mul)

claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hpNonzero : p <> ring_zero K add.
exact (andER
(p :e K)
(p <> ring_zero K add)
(andEL
(p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
(not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(andEL
((p :e K /\ p <> ring_zero K add)
/\ not (ring_unit K add mul p))
(forall d :e K,
ring_divides K mul d p ->
ring_unit K add mul d
\/ exists u :e K, ring_unit K add mul u /\ d = mul u p)
hPExtremal))).

let z.
assume hz.

(ring_one K mul :e K)

mul w (ring_one K mul) = w /\ mul (ring_one K mul) w = w)

(ring_nat_power K add mul p 0 :e K) (z :e K)

(fun c => c :e K
/\ z = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p 0))
z
(andI
(z :e K)
(z = mul z (ring_nat_power K add mul p 0))
hz hZEquation))).

(0 = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)

\/ ring_divides K mul p b.

K add mul p hp a ha b hb hPID hPExtremal hPDividesAB).
claim hLeftCase : ring_divides K mul p a ->
exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)

(p :e K /\ a :e K)
(exists a1 :e K, a = mul a1 p) hPDividesA).

let a1.
assume ha1Data.
claim ha1 : a1 :e K.
exact (andEL (a1 :e K) (a = mul a1 p) ha1Data).
claim hAFactor : a = mul a1 p.
exact (andER (a1 :e K) (a = mul a1 p) ha1Data).
claim hResidualDivides : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a1 b).
exact (god1_cancel_power_from_divided_product_factor
K add mul hIntegral p hp a ha a1 ha1 b hb r
(nat_p_omega r hr) hpNonzero hAFactor hPowerDividesAB).
claim hInductionResult : exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
exact (hInduction a1 ha1 b hb hResidualDivides).
apply hInductionResult.
let s.
assume hsData.
claim hs : s :e omega.
exact (andEL
(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hsData).
claim hTExists : exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
exact (andER
(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hsData).
apply hTExists.
let t.
assume htData.
claim ht : t :e omega.
exact (andEL
(t :e omega)
((r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
htData).
claim hSTBody :
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
exact (andER
(t :e omega)
((r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
htData).
claim hSTPrefix : r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1.
exact (andEL
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hSTBody).
claim hRSum : r = add_nat s t.
exact (andEL
(r = add_nat s t)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
hSTPrefix).
claim hPowerSDividesA1 : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1.
exact (andER
(r = add_nat s t)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
hSTPrefix).
claim hPowerTDividesB : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
exact (andER
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a1)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hSTBody).
claim hPowerSuccSDividesA : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a.
exact (god1_power_successor_divides_after_restoring_factor
K add mul hRing p hp a ha a1 ha1 s hs hAFactor hPowerSDividesA1).
claim hSuccessorSum : ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t.
exact (eq_i_tra
(ordsucc r) (ordsucc (add_nat s t)) (add_nat (ordsucc s) t)
(f_eq_i ordsucc r (add_nat s t) hRSum)
(eq_sym
(add_nat (ordsucc s) t) (ordsucc (add_nat s t))
(add_nat_SL s (omega_nat_p s hs) t (omega_nat_p t ht)))).
exact (ex_intro
(fun s0 => s0 :e omega /\ exists t0 :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s0 t0
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s0) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b)
(ordsucc s)
(andI
(ordsucc s :e omega)
(exists t0 :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t0
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b)
(omega_ordsucc s hs)
(ex_intro
(fun t0 => t0 :e omega /\
((ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t0
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b))
t
(andI
(t :e omega)
((ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
ht
(andI
(ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
(andI
(ordsucc r = add_nat (ordsucc s) t)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc s)) a)
hSuccessorSum hPowerSuccSDividesA)
hPowerTDividesB))))).
claim hRightCase : ring_divides K mul p b ->
exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
assume hPDividesB.
claim hB1Exists : exists b1 :e K, b = mul b1 p.
exact (andER
(p :e K /\ b :e K)
(exists b1 :e K, b = mul b1 p) hPDividesB).
apply hB1Exists.
let b1.
assume hb1Data.
claim hb1 : b1 :e K.
exact (andEL (b1 :e K) (b = mul b1 p) hb1Data).
claim hBFactor : b = mul b1 p.
exact (andER (b1 :e K) (b = mul b1 p) hb1Data).
claim hBAEq : mul b a = mul a b.
exact (hComm b hb a ha).
claim hPowerDividesBA : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)) (mul b a).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)) z)
(mul a b) (mul b a)
(eq_sym (mul b a) (mul a b) hBAEq)
hPowerDividesAB).
claim hResidualBA : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul b1 a).
exact (god1_cancel_power_from_divided_product_factor
K add mul hIntegral p hp b hb b1 hb1 a ha r
(nat_p_omega r hr) hpNonzero hBFactor hPowerDividesBA).
claim hB1AEq : mul b1 a = mul a b1.
exact (hComm b1 hb1 a ha).
claim hResidualDivides : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a b1).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) z)
(mul b1 a) (mul a b1) hB1AEq hResidualBA).
claim hInductionResult : exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1.
exact (hInduction a ha b1 hb1 hResidualDivides).
apply hInductionResult.
let s.
assume hsData.
claim hs : s :e omega.
exact (andEL
(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
hsData).
claim hTExists : exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1.
exact (andER
(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
hsData).
apply hTExists.
let t.
assume htData.
claim ht : t :e omega.
exact (andEL
(t :e omega)
((r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
htData).
claim hSTBody :
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1.
exact (andER
(t :e omega)
((r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
htData).
claim hSTPrefix : r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a.
exact (andEL
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
hSTBody).
claim hRSum : r = add_nat s t.
exact (andEL
(r = add_nat s t)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
hSTPrefix).
claim hPowerSDividesA : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a.
exact (andER
(r = add_nat s t)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
hSTPrefix).
claim hPowerTDividesB1 : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1.
exact (andER
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b1)
hSTBody).
claim hPowerSuccTDividesB : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc t)) b.
exact (god1_power_successor_divides_after_restoring_factor
K add mul hRing p hp b hb b1 hb1 t ht hBFactor hPowerTDividesB1).
claim hSuccessorSum : ordsucc r = add_nat s (ordsucc t).
exact (eq_i_tra
(ordsucc r) (ordsucc (add_nat s t)) (add_nat s (ordsucc t))
(f_eq_i ordsucc r (add_nat s t) hRSum)
(eq_sym
(add_nat s (ordsucc t)) (ordsucc (add_nat s t))
(add_nat_SR s t (omega_nat_p t ht)))).
exact (ex_intro
(fun s0 => s0 :e omega /\ exists t0 :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s0 t0
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s0) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b)
s
(andI
(s :e omega)
(exists t0 :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s t0
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b)
hs
(ex_intro
(fun t0 => t0 :e omega /\
((ordsucc r = add_nat s t0
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t0) b))
(ordsucc t)
(andI
(ordsucc t :e omega)
((ordsucc r = add_nat s (ordsucc t)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc t)) b)
(omega_ordsucc t ht)
(andI
(ordsucc r = add_nat s (ordsucc t)
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc t)) b)
(andI
(ordsucc r = add_nat s (ordsucc t))
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
hSuccessorSum hPowerSDividesA)
hPowerSuccTDividesB))))).
exact (orE
(ring_divides K mul p a) (ring_divides K mul p b)
hFactorCases
(exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(ordsucc r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hLeftCase hRightCase).
claim hAll : forall r, nat_p r -> forall a b :e K,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a b) ->
exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b.
exact (nat_ind
(fun r => forall a b :e K,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul a b) ->
exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,
(r = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) a)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) b)
hBase hStep).
let r.
assume hr.
let a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb hPowerDivides.
exact (hAll r (omega_nat_p r hr) a ha b hb hPowerDivides).
Qed.

Theorem god1_product_of_divisible_extremal_powers :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
commutative_ring K add mul -> forall p x y :e K,
forall s t :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x ->
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y ->
ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)) (mul x y).
let K add mul.
assume hCommRing.
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let s.
assume hs.
let t.
assume ht hPowerSDividesX hPowerTDividesY.
claim hPowerSIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p s :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp s hs).
claim hPowerTIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p t :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp t ht).
claim hPowerSumIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp
(add_nat s t)
(nat_p_omega (add_nat s t)
(add_nat_p s (omega_nat_p s hs) t (omega_nat_p t ht)))).
claim hCExists : exists c :e K,
x = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s).
exact (andER
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s :e K /\ x :e K)
(exists c :e K, x = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s))
hPowerSDividesX).
apply hCExists.
let c.
assume hcData.
claim hc : c :e K.
exact (andEL
(c :e K)
(x = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s)) hcData).
claim hXEquation : x = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s).
exact (andER
(c :e K)
(x = mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s)) hcData).
claim hDExists : exists d :e K,
y = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t).
exact (andER
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t :e K /\ y :e K)
(exists d :e K, y = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t))
hPowerTDividesY).
apply hDExists.
let d.
assume hdData.
claim hd : d :e K.
exact (andEL
(d :e K)
(y = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t)) hdData).
claim hYEquation : y = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t).
exact (andER
(d :e K)
(y = mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t)) hdData).
claim hPowerProduct :
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t)
= ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t).
exact (god1_ring_natural_power_add K add mul hRing
p hp s hs t ht).
claim hProductEquation : mul x y
= mul (mul c d) (ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul x y)
(mul
(mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s))
(mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t)))
(mul (mul c d) (ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)))
(god1_binary_operation_congruence mul
x (mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s))
y (mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t))
hXEquation hYEquation)
(eq_i_tra
(mul
(mul c (ring_nat_power K add mul p s))
(mul d (ring_nat_power K add mul p t)))
(mul (mul c d)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t)))
(mul (mul c d) (ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)))
(god1_commutative_ring_four_factor_interchange
K add mul hCommRing c hc
(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) hPowerSIn
d hd (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) hPowerTIn)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul (mul c d) z)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p t))
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)) hPowerProduct))).
claim hCDIn : mul c d :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing c hc d hd).
claim hXYIn : mul x y :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing x hx y hy).
exact (andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t) :e K /\ mul x y :e K)
(exists q :e K,
mul x y = mul q (ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)))
(andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t) :e K)
(mul x y :e K) hPowerSumIn hXYIn)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K
/\ mul x y = mul q
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)))
(mul c d)
(andI
(mul c d :e K)
(mul x y = mul (mul c d)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (add_nat s t)))
hCDIn hProductEquation))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y)
= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let K add mul.
let p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero hyNonzero.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hXYIn : mul x y :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing x hx y hy).
claim hXYNonzero : mul x y <> ring_zero K add.
assume hXYZero.
claim hZeroCases : x = ring_zero K add \/ y = ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_zero_product K add mul hIntegral
x hx y hy hXYZero).
exact (orE
(x = ring_zero K add) (y = ring_zero K add) hZeroCases False
hxNonzero hyNonzero).
claim hXSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hYSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) y ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp y hy hPID hPExtremal hyNonzero).
claim hXYSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y))) (mul x y))
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) (mul x y) ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y).
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp (mul x y) hXYIn
hPID hPExtremal hXYNonzero).
claim hXPrefix : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hXSpec).
claim hValXIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hXPrefix).
claim hValXDivides : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hXPrefix).
claim hXMaximal : forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hXSpec).
claim hYPrefix : extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) y ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
hYSpec).
claim hValYIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y)
hYPrefix).
claim hValYDivides : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)) y.
exact (andER

hYPrefix).

(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y))) (mul x y).

claim hSplitExists : exists s :e omega, exists t :e omega,

/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y.

(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,

/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y)
hsData).
claim hTExists : exists t :e omega,
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y.
exact (andER
(s :e omega)
(exists t :e omega,
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t

/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y)
hsData).
apply hTExists.
let t.
assume htData.
claim ht : t :e omega.
exact (andEL
(t :e omega)
((extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y)
htData).
claim hSTBody :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x)
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y.
exact (andER
(t :e omega)
((extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t

/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y)
htData).
claim hSTPrefix :
extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x.

(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t

= add_nat s t.

(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x)

(ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x.

(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t)

(ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y.

(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y) = add_nat s t
/\ ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p s) x)
(ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p t) y)
hSTBody).
claim hSBound : s c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (hXMaximal s hs hSDividesX).
claim hTBound : t c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (hYMaximal t ht hTDividesY).
claim hFirstAddBound : add_nat s t c= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) t.
exact (add_nat_Subq_R
s (omega_nat_p s hs)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(omega_nat_p (extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValXIn)
hSBound t (omega_nat_p t ht)).
claim hSecondAddBound : add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) t
c= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
exact (add_nat_Subq_L
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(omega_nat_p (extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValXIn)
t (omega_nat_p t ht)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(omega_nat_p (extremal_valuation K add mul p y) hValYIn)
hTBound).
claim hSTBound : add_nat s t c= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
exact (Subq_tra
(add_nat s t)
(add_nat (extremal_valuation K add mul p x) t)
(add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
hFirstAddBound hSecondAddBound).
claim hUpperBound : extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y)
c= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => z c= add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
(add_nat s t)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y))
(eq_sym
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y))
(add_nat s t) hSplitEquation)
hSTBound).
exact (set_ext
(extremal_valuation K add mul p (mul x y))
(add_nat
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
hUpperBound hLowerBound).
Qed.

Theorem god1_natural_add_right_subset_cancel :
forall a b c :e omega,
add_nat a c c= add_nat b c -> a c= b.
let a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb.
let c.
assume hc hAddSub.
claim hAddAIn : add_nat a c :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega (add_nat a c)
(add_nat_p a (omega_nat_p a ha) c (omega_nat_p c hc))).
claim hAddBIn : add_nat b c :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega (add_nat b c)
(add_nat_p b (omega_nat_p b hb) c (omega_nat_p c hc))).
claim hNaturalLe : add_nat a c <= add_nat b c.
exact (omega_Subq_SNoLe
(add_nat a c) hAddAIn (add_nat b c) hAddBIn hAddSub).
claim hRightRewritten : add_nat a c <= add_SNo b c.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => add_nat a c <= z)
(add_nat b c) (add_SNo b c)
(add_nat_add_SNo b hb c hc) hNaturalLe).
claim hSurrealLe : add_SNo a c <= add_SNo b c.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => z <= add_SNo b c)
(add_nat a c) (add_SNo a c)
(add_nat_add_SNo a ha c hc) hRightRewritten).
claim hACancelled : a <= b.
exact (add_SNo_Le1_cancel a c b
(omega_SNo a ha) (omega_SNo c hc) (omega_SNo b hb)
hSurrealLe).
exact (omega_SNoLe_Subq a ha b hb hACancelled).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_positive_of_divides :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add ->
ring_divides K mul p x ->
1 c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
let K add mul.
let p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero hPDividesX.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hPowerOne : ring_nat_power K add mul p 1 = p.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_one K add mul hRing p hp).
claim hPowerOneDividesX : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p 1) x.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun d => ring_divides K mul d x)
p (ring_nat_power K add mul p 1)
(eq_sym (ring_nat_power K add mul p 1) p hPowerOne)
hPDividesX).
claim hSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hMaximal : forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hSpec).
exact (hMaximal 1 (nat_p_omega 1 nat_1) hPowerOneDividesX).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_divides_of_positive_valuation :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add ->
1 c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x ->
ring_divides K mul p x.
let K add mul.
let p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero hPositive.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hSpec :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
/\ forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hPrefix : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hSpec).
claim hValIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hPrefix).
claim hValPowerDividesX : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hPrefix).
claim hZeroInValuation : 0 :e extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (hPositive 0 In_0_1).
claim hSuccessorExists : exists r,
nat_p r /\ extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r.
claim hCases : extremal_valuation K add mul p x = 0
\/ exists r, nat_p r
/\ extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r.
exact (nat_inv
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(omega_nat_p (extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValIn)).
exact (orE
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x = 0)
(exists r, nat_p r
/\ extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r)
hCases
(exists r, nat_p r
/\ extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r)
(fun hZero => FalseE
(EmptyE 0
(mem_eq_set_subst
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) 0 0
hZero hZeroInValuation))
(exists r, nat_p r
/\ extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r))
(fun hExists => hExists)).
apply hSuccessorExists.
let r.
assume hrData.
claim hr : nat_p r.
exact (andEL
(nat_p r)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r) hrData).
claim hValEq : extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r.
exact (andER
(nat_p r)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x = ordsucc r) hrData).
claim hPowerRIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp r
(nat_p_omega r hr)).
claim hPowerSuccIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp
(ordsucc r) (nat_p_omega (ordsucc r) (nat_ordsucc r hr))).
claim hPowerSuccessor : ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)
= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_successor K add mul p r hr).
claim hPDividesSuccessorPower : ring_divides K mul p
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)).
exact (andI
(p :e K /\ ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) :e K)
(exists c :e K,
ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) = mul c p)
(andI
(p :e K)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) :e K)
hp hPowerSuccIn)
(ex_intro
(fun c => c :e K
/\ ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r) = mul c p)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r)
(andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)
= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) p)
hPowerRIn hPowerSuccessor))).
claim hSuccessorPowerDividesX : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)) x.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun d => ring_divides K mul d x)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x))
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r))
(f_eq_i (fun n => ring_nat_power K add mul p n)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) (ordsucc r) hValEq)
hValPowerDividesX).
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
p hp
(ring_nat_power K add mul p (ordsucc r)) hPowerSuccIn
x hx hPDividesSuccessorPower hSuccessorPowerDividesX).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_unit_divides_every_element :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall u x :e K,
ring_unit K add mul u -> ring_divides K mul u x.
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let u.
assume hu.
let x.
assume hx hUnitU.
claim hOneIn : ring_one K mul :e K.
exact (andEL
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing)).
claim hInverseExists : exists v :e K,
mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(u :e K)
(exists v :e K,
mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hUnitU).
apply hInverseExists.
let v.
assume hvData.
claim hv : v :e K.
exact (andEL
(v :e K)
(mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hvData).
claim hInverseBody : mul v u = ring_one K mul
/\ mul u v = ring_one K mul.
exact (andER
(v :e K)
(mul v u = ring_one K mul /\ mul u v = ring_one K mul)
hvData).
claim hVUTimes : mul v u = ring_one K mul.
exact (andEL
(mul v u = ring_one K mul)
(mul u v = ring_one K mul) hInverseBody).
claim hRightIdentity : mul x (ring_one K mul) = x.
exact (andEL
(mul x (ring_one K mul) = x)
(mul (ring_one K mul) x = x)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z /\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification K add mul hRing))
x hx)).
claim hQuotientIn : mul x v :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing x hx v hv).
claim hQuotientEquation : x = mul (mul x v) u.
exact (eq_sym
(mul (mul x v) u) x
(eq_i_tra
(mul (mul x v) u) (mul x (mul v u)) x
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative_reverse
K add mul hRing x hx v hv u hu)
(eq_i_tra
(mul x (mul v u))
(mul x (ring_one K mul)) x
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul x z)
(mul v u) (ring_one K mul) hVUTimes)
hRightIdentity))).
exact (andI
(u :e K /\ x :e K)
(exists q :e K, x = mul q u)
(andI
(u :e K) (x :e K) hu hx)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K /\ x = mul q u)
(mul x v)
(andI
(mul x v :e K) (x = mul (mul x v) u)
hQuotientIn hQuotientEquation))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_bounds_imply_divisibility :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y) ->
ring_divides K mul x y.
let K add mul.
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hBounds.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hBase : forall u :e K, forall f :e K :^: 0,
ring_unit K add mul u ->
(forall i :e 0, extremal_element K add mul (f i)) ->
forall z :e K,
mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => f i))
<> ring_zero K add ->
z <> ring_zero K add ->
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => f i)))
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p z) ->
ring_divides K mul
(mul u (ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => f i))) z.
let u.
assume hu.
let f.
assume hf hUnitU hEmptyExtremal.
let z.
assume hz hExpressionNonzero hzNonzero hEmptyBounds.
claim hEmptyProduct : ring_finite_product K add mul 0 (fun i => f i)
= ring_one K mul.
exact (god1_ring_finite_product_empty K add mul (fun i => f i)).

Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_divisibility_iff_bounds :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall x y :e K,

x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->

<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero.
apply iffI.
- assume hDivides.
let p.
assume hp hPExtremal.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_monotone_under_divisibility
K add mul p hp x hx y hy hPID hPExtremal
hxNonzero hyNonzero hDivides).
- assume hBounds.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_bounds_imply_divisibility
K add mul x hx y hy hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hBounds).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma4_divisibility_by_extremal_valuations :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set, forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
(ring_divides K mul x y
<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hxne hyne.

(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).

exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
//GOD1PRF:957087 lemma 4. Let $x, y$ be two non-zero elements of K . Then $x$ divides $y$ if and only if

ring_divides K mul x y
<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_divisibility_iff_bounds
K add mul x hx y hy hPID hxne hyne).

(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y) ->
ring_divides K mul x y.

(ring_divides K mul x y)
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
h_s31_l4_statement).
//GOD1PRF:957470 are all $\geqslant 0$ and almost all are 0 ; so that $y=x z$, where
claim h_s31_l4_quotient_exists :
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y) ->
exists z :e K, y = mul x z.

claim hRawQuotient : exists z :e K, y = mul z x.

(x :e K /\ y :e K)
(exists z :e K, y = mul z x)
hDivides).
apply hRawQuotient.
let z.
assume hzData.
claim hz : z :e K.
exact (andEL (z :e K) (y = mul z x) hzData).
claim hRawEquation : y = mul z x.
exact (andER (z :e K) (y = mul z x) hzData).
claim hCommutedEquation : y = mul x z.

hRawEquation (hComm z hz x hx)).
exact (ex_intro
(fun z => z :e K /\ y = mul x z)
z
(andI (z :e K) (y = mul x z) hz hCommutedEquation)).
//GOD1PRF:957595 Conversely, suppose that $y=x z$. Then, using the prime factorizations of $x$ and $z$, we have
claim h_s31_l4_necessity : ring_divides K mul x y ->
forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y.

(ring_divides K mul x y)

h_s31_l4_statement).
//GOD1PRF:957734 where $u$ is a unit. Since the decomposition of $y$ as the product of a unit and elements of P is unique, we see that $v_{p}(y)=v_{p}(x)+v_{p}(z)$, and therefore $v_{p}(y) \geqslant v_{p}(x)$ for all $p \in \mathrm{P}$. This completes the proof of Lemma 4.
claim h_s31_l4_theorem7_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall x0 :e K0, forall m0 n0 :e omega,
forall p0 :e K0 :^: m0, forall q0 :e K0 :^: n0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> not (ring_unit K0 add0 mul0 x0) ->
(forall i :e m0, extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 (p0 i)) ->
(forall j :e n0, extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 (q0 j)) ->
x0 = ring_finite_product K0 add0 mul0 m0 (fun i => p0 i) ->
x0 = ring_finite_product K0 add0 mul0 n0 (fun j => q0 j) ->
m0 = n0
/\ exists sigma :e permutation_group n0,
forall i :e n0, associated_elements K0 add0 mul0 (p0 i) (q0 (sigma i)).
apply god1_s31_theorem7_uniqueness_of_extremal_factorization.
claim h_s31_l4_conclusion :
ring_divides K mul x y
<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact h_s31_l4_statement.
exact h_s31_l4_conclusion.
Qed.

//GOD1:958268 natural_minimum : "the minimum of natural numbers #1 and #2" | $\min(#1,#2)$
Definition natural_minimum : set -> set -> set :=
fun n m => if n c= m then n else m.

//GOD1:958268 natural_maximum : "the maximum of natural numbers #1 and #2" | $\max(#1,#2)$
Definition natural_maximum : set -> set -> set :=
fun n m => if n c= m then m else n.

Theorem god1_natural_minimum_in_and_bounds :
forall a b :e omega,
(natural_minimum a b :e omega
/\ natural_minimum a b c= a)
/\ natural_minimum a b c= b.
let a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb.
claim hOrdA : ordinal a.
exact (nat_p_ordinal a (omega_nat_p a ha)).
claim hOrdB : ordinal b.
exact (nat_p_ordinal b (omega_nat_p b hb)).
apply (orE
(a c= b) (not (a c= b)) (xm (a c= b))
((natural_minimum a b :e omega
/\ natural_minimum a b c= a)
/\ natural_minimum a b c= b)).
- assume hab.
claim hMinimum : natural_minimum a b = a.
exact (If_i_1 (a c= b) a b hab).
claim hMinimumIn : natural_minimum a b :e omega.
exact (mem_eq_substL omega a (natural_minimum a b)
hMinimum ha).
claim hMinimumA : natural_minimum a b c= a.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun q => q c= a) a (natural_minimum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_minimum a b) a hMinimum)
(Subq_ref a)).
claim hMinimumB : natural_minimum a b c= b.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun q => q c= b) a (natural_minimum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_minimum a b) a hMinimum) hab).
exact (andI
(natural_minimum a b :e omega
/\ natural_minimum a b c= a)
(natural_minimum a b c= b)
(andI
(natural_minimum a b :e omega)
(natural_minimum a b c= a)
hMinimumIn hMinimumA)
hMinimumB).
- assume hnab.
claim hba : b c= a.
exact (orE
(a c= b) (b c= a) (ordinal_linear a b hOrdA hOrdB)
(b c= a)
(fun hab => FalseE (hnab hab) (b c= a))
(fun hba => hba)).
claim hMinimum : natural_minimum a b = b.
exact (If_i_0 (a c= b) a b hnab).
claim hMinimumIn : natural_minimum a b :e omega.
exact (mem_eq_substL omega b (natural_minimum a b)
hMinimum hb).
claim hMinimumA : natural_minimum a b c= a.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun q => q c= a) b (natural_minimum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_minimum a b) b hMinimum) hba).
claim hMinimumB : natural_minimum a b c= b.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun q => q c= b) b (natural_minimum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_minimum a b) b hMinimum)
(Subq_ref b)).
exact (andI
(natural_minimum a b :e omega
/\ natural_minimum a b c= a)
(natural_minimum a b c= b)
(andI
(natural_minimum a b :e omega)
(natural_minimum a b c= a)
hMinimumIn hMinimumA)
hMinimumB).
Qed.

(fun q => q c= r) b (natural_maximum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_maximum a b) b
(If_i_1 (a c= b) b a hab)) hbr).
- assume hnab.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun q => q c= r) a (natural_maximum a b)
(eq_sym (natural_maximum a b) a
(If_i_0 (a c= b) b a hnab)) har).
Qed.

Theorem god1_natural_minimum_maximum_sum :
forall a b :e omega,
add_nat a b = add_nat
(natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b).
let a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb.
apply (orE
(a c= b) (not (a c= b)) (xm (a c= b))
(add_nat a b = add_nat
(natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b))).
- assume hab.
claim hMinimum : natural_minimum a b = a.
exact (If_i_1 (a c= b) a b hab).
claim hMaximum : natural_maximum a b = b.
exact (If_i_1 (a c= b) b a hab).
claim hRight : add_nat
(natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b) = add_nat b a.
exact (god1_binary_operation_congruence add_nat
(natural_maximum a b) b
(natural_minimum a b) a hMaximum hMinimum).
exact (eq_i_tra
(add_nat a b) (add_nat b a)
(add_nat (natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b))
(add_nat_com a (omega_nat_p a ha) b (omega_nat_p b hb))
(eq_sym
(add_nat (natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b))
(add_nat b a) hRight)).
- assume hnab.
claim hMinimum : natural_minimum a b = b.
exact (If_i_0 (a c= b) a b hnab).
claim hMaximum : natural_maximum a b = a.
exact (If_i_0 (a c= b) b a hnab).
exact (eq_sym
(add_nat (natural_maximum a b) (natural_minimum a b))
(add_nat a b)
(god1_binary_operation_congruence add_nat
(natural_maximum a b) a
(natural_minimum a b) b hMaximum hMinimum)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_integral_domain_nonzero_product :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul -> forall x y :e K,
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
mul x y <> ring_zero K add.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hNoZeroDivisors : forall u v :e K,
mul u v = ring_zero K add ->
u = ring_zero K add \/ v = ring_zero K add.
exact (andER
(commutative_ring K add mul
/\ ring_one K mul <> ring_zero K add)
(forall u v :e K,
mul u v = ring_zero K add ->
u = ring_zero K add \/ v = ring_zero K add)
hIntegral).
let x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hxNonzero hyNonzero hProductZero.
exact (orE
(x = ring_zero K add) (y = ring_zero K add)
(hNoZeroDivisors x hx y hy hProductZero)
False hxNonzero hyNonzero).
Qed.

Theorem god1_nonzero_multiple_has_nonzero_divisor :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall d x :e K,
x <> ring_zero K add -> ring_divides K mul d x ->
d <> ring_zero K add.
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let d.
assume hd.
let x.
assume hx hxNonzero hDivides hdZero.
claim hQuotientExists : exists q :e K, x = mul q d.
exact (andER
(d :e K /\ x :e K)
(exists q :e K, x = mul q d)
hDivides).
apply hQuotientExists.
let q.
assume hqData.
claim hq : q :e K.
exact (andEL (q :e K) (x = mul q d) hqData).
claim hEquation : x = mul q d.
exact (andER (q :e K) (x = mul q d) hqData).
exact (hxNonzero
(eq_i_tra x (mul q d) (ring_zero K add)
hEquation
(eq_i_tra
(mul q d) (mul q (ring_zero K add)) (ring_zero K add)
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul q z) d (ring_zero K add) hdZero)
(god1_ring_zero_multiplication_right
K add mul hRing q hq)))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_principal_ideals_equal_of_mutual_divisibility :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall d e :e K,
ring_divides K mul d e -> ring_divides K mul e d ->
principal_ideal K add mul d = principal_ideal K add mul e.
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let d.
assume hd.
let e.
assume he hDDividesE hEDividesD.
claim hDSubsetK : principal_ideal K add mul d c= K.
exact (god1_subgroup_subset K add
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_principal_ideal_additive_subgroup
K add mul d hd hRing)).
claim hESubsetK : principal_ideal K add mul e c= K.
exact (god1_subgroup_subset K add
(principal_ideal K add mul e)
(god1_principal_ideal_additive_subgroup
K add mul e he hRing)).
apply set_ext.
- let z.
assume hzD.
claim hz : z :e K.
exact (hDSubsetK z hzD).
claim hDDividesZ : ring_divides K mul d z.
exact (iffER
(ring_divides K mul d z)
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd z hz) hzD).
claim hEDividesZ : ring_divides K mul e z.
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
e he d hd z hz hEDividesD hDDividesZ).
exact (iffEL
(ring_divides K mul e z)
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul e)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing e he z hz) hEDividesZ).
- let z.
assume hzE.
claim hz : z :e K.
exact (hESubsetK z hzE).
claim hEDividesZ : ring_divides K mul e z.
exact (iffER
(ring_divides K mul e z)
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul e)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing e he z hz) hzE).
claim hDDividesZ : ring_divides K mul d z.
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
d hd e he z hz hDDividesE hEDividesZ).
exact (iffEL
(ring_divides K mul d z)
(z :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd z hz) hDDividesZ).
Qed.

Theorem god1_mutual_divisibility_of_equal_principal_ideals :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall d e :e K,
principal_ideal K add mul d = principal_ideal K add mul e ->
ring_divides K mul d e /\ ring_divides K mul e d.
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let d.
assume hd.
let e.
assume he hPrincipalEq.
claim hdInD : d :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_contains_generator
K add mul hRing d hd).
claim heInE : e :e principal_ideal K add mul e.
exact (god1_principal_ideal_contains_generator
K add mul hRing e he).
claim heInD : e :e principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul e)
(principal_ideal K add mul d) e
(eq_sym
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul e) hPrincipalEq)
heInE).
claim hdInE : d :e principal_ideal K add mul e.
exact (mem_eq_set_subst
(principal_ideal K add mul d)
(principal_ideal K add mul e) d hPrincipalEq hdInD).
exact (andI
(ring_divides K mul d e)
(ring_divides K mul e d)
(iffER
(ring_divides K mul d e)
(e :e principal_ideal K add mul d)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing d hd e he) heInD)
(iffER
(ring_divides K mul e d)
(d :e principal_ideal K add mul e)
(god1_ring_divides_iff_principal_ideal_membership
K add mul hRing e he d hd) hdInE)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_valuations_equal_of_mutual_divisibility :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall a b :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
a <> ring_zero K add -> b <> ring_zero K add ->

extremal_valuation K add mul p a
= extremal_valuation K add mul p b.

let b.
assume hb hPID haNonzero hbNonzero hADividesB hBDividesA.
let p.

haNonzero hbNonzero hADividesB)
(god1_extremal_valuation_monotone_under_divisibility
K add mul p hp b hb a ha hPID hPExtremal
hbNonzero haNonzero hBDividesA)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_nat_power_addition :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall x :e K, forall r s :e omega,
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s).
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let x.
assume hx.
let r.
assume hr.
claim hPowerRIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx r hr).
claim hBase :
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x 0)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r 0).
claim hRightIdentity :
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) (ring_one K mul)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x r.
exact (andEL
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) (ring_one K mul)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(mul (ring_one K mul) (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
((andER
(ring_one K mul :e K)
(forall z :e K,
mul z (ring_one K mul) = z
/\ mul (ring_one K mul) z = z)
(god1_ring_multiplicative_identity_specification
K add mul hRing))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r) hPowerRIn)).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x 0))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) (ring_one K mul))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r 0))
(f_eq_i
(fun z => mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) z)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x 0) (ring_one K mul)
(god1_ring_nat_power_zero K add mul x))
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) (ring_one K mul))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r 0))
hRightIdentity
(f_eq_i (fun q => ring_nat_power K add mul x q)
r (add_nat r 0) (eq_sym (add_nat r 0) r (add_nat_0R r))))).
claim hStep : forall s, nat_p s ->
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s) ->
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc s))
= ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r (ordsucc s)).
let s.
assume hs hInduction.
claim hsOmega : s :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega s hs).
claim hPowerSIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x s :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx s hsOmega).
exact (eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc s)))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x s) x))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r (ordsucc s)))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) z)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc s))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x s) x)
(god1_ring_nat_power_successor K add mul x s hs))
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x s) x))
(mul
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s)) x)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r (ordsucc s)))
(god1_ring_multiplicative_associative K add mul hRing
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r) hPowerRIn
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s) hPowerSIn x hx)
(eq_i_tra
(mul
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s)) x)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s)) x)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r (ordsucc s)))
(f_eq_i (fun z => mul z x)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s)) hInduction)
(eq_i_tra
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s)) x)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc (add_nat r s)))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r (ordsucc s)))
(eq_sym
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc (add_nat r s)))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r s)) x)
(god1_ring_nat_power_successor K add mul x
(add_nat r s)
(add_nat_p r (omega_nat_p r hr) s hs)))
(f_eq_i (fun q => ring_nat_power K add mul x q)
(ordsucc (add_nat r s)) (add_nat r (ordsucc s))
(eq_sym
(add_nat r (ordsucc s)) (ordsucc (add_nat r s))
(add_nat_SR r s hs))))))).
let s.
assume hs.
exact (nat_ind
(fun q =>
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x q)
= ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat r q))
hBase hStep s (omega_nat_p s hs)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_ring_nat_power_divides_of_exponent_subset :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
ring K add mul -> forall x :e K, forall r s :e omega,
r c= s ->
ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s).
let K add mul.
assume hRing.
let x.
assume hx.
let r.
assume hr.
let s.
assume hs hrs.
claim hDifferenceExists : exists k,
nat_p k /\ s = add_nat k r.
exact (nat_Subq_add_ex r (omega_nat_p r hr)
s (omega_nat_p s hs) hrs).
apply hDifferenceExists.
let k.
assume hkData.
claim hkNat : nat_p k.
exact (andEL (nat_p k) (s = add_nat k r) hkData).
claim hk : k :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega k hkNat).
claim hExponent : s = add_nat k r.
exact (andER (nat_p k) (s = add_nat k r) hkData).
claim hPowerRIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx r hr).
claim hPowerSIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x s :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx s hs).
claim hPowerKIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x k :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx k hk).
claim hFactorization : ring_nat_power K add mul x s
= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x k)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r).
exact (eq_i_tra
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat k r))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x k)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
(f_eq_i (fun q => ring_nat_power K add mul x q)
s (add_nat k r) hExponent)
(eq_sym
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x k)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (add_nat k r))
(god1_ring_nat_power_addition
K add mul hRing x hx k hk r hr))).
exact (andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r :e K
/\ ring_nat_power K add mul x s :e K)
(exists q :e K,
ring_nat_power K add mul x s
= mul q (ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
(andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r :e K)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s :e K)
hPowerRIn hPowerSIn)
(ex_intro
(fun q => q :e K
/\ ring_nat_power K add mul x s
= mul q (ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
(ring_nat_power K add mul x k)
(andI
(ring_nat_power K add mul x k :e K)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x s
= mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x k)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
hPowerKIn hFactorization))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_valuation_in :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.

let x.

exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall r :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_extremal_power_divides_at_most_valuation :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall p x :e K, forall r :e omega,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
extremal_element K add mul p ->
x <> ring_zero K add ->
r c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x ->
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p r) x.
let K add mul p.
assume hp.
let x.
assume hx.
let r.
assume hr hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero hBound.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hSpecification :
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
/\ forall q :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p q) x ->
q c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_specification
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hValuationAndPower :
extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega
/\ ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
(forall q :e omega,
ring_divides K mul (ring_nat_power K add mul p q) x ->
q c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
hSpecification).
claim hValuationIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.
exact (andEL
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hValuationAndPower).
claim hMaximalPowerDivides : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x.
exact (andER
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega)
(ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) x)
hValuationAndPower).
claim hLowerPowerDividesMaximal : ring_divides K mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)).
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_divides_of_exponent_subset
K add mul hRing p hp r hr
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValuationIn hBound).
claim hLowerPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp r hr).
claim hMaximalPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing p hp
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValuationIn).
exact (god1_ring_divides_transitive K add mul hRing
(ring_nat_power K add mul p r) hLowerPowerIn
(ring_nat_power K add mul p
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)) hMaximalPowerIn
x hx hLowerPowerDividesMaximal hMaximalPowerDivides).
Qed.

Theorem god1_two_element_hcf_extremal_valuation_minimum :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y d :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d ->
d <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p d
= natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let d.
assume hd hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hHcf.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hTwoOmega : 2 :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega 2 nat_2).
claim hFamilyMaps : forall i :e 2,
(if i = 0 then x else y) :e K.
let i.
assume hi.
exact (cases_2 i hi
(fun j => (if j = 0 then x else y) :e K)
(mem_eq_substL K x (if 0 = 0 then x else y)
(If_i_1 (0 = 0) x y (eq_ref 0)) hx)
(mem_eq_substL K y (if 1 = 0 then x else y)
(If_i_0 (1 = 0) x y neq_1_0) hy)).
claim hFamily :
(fun i :e 2 => if i = 0 then x else y) :e K :^: 2.
exact (lam_Pi 2 (fun i => K)
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) hFamilyMaps).
claim hIdealRaw :
ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y)
= principal_ideal K add mul d.
exact (andER
(d :e K)
(ideal_generated_by_finite_family K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y)
= principal_ideal K add mul d)
hHcf).

Theorem god1_two_element_lcm_extremal_valuation_maximum :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y m :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m ->
m <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p m
= natural_maximum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let m.
assume hm hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hLcm.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hProductIn : mul x y :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law
K add mul hRing x hx y hy).
claim hProductNonzero : mul x y <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_nonzero_product
K add mul hIntegral x hx y hy hxNonzero hyNonzero).
claim hPairExists : exists d0 m0 :e K,
highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d0
/\ least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m0
/\ mul x y = mul m0 d0.
exact (god1_s31_theorem3_hcf_lcm_product

apply hPairExists.
let d0.
assume hd0Data.
claim hd0 : d0 :e K.
exact (andEL
(d0 :e K)

Theorem god1_common_divisor_iff_extremal_valuation_minimum_bound :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y z :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
z <> ring_zero K add ->
((ring_divides K mul z x /\ ring_divides K mul z y)
<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let z.
assume hz hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hzNonzero.
apply iffI.
- assume hCommon.
claim hZDividesX : ring_divides K mul z x.
exact (andEL
(ring_divides K mul z x)
(ring_divides K mul z y) hCommon).
claim hZDividesY : ring_divides K mul z y.
exact (andER
(ring_divides K mul z x)
(ring_divides K mul z y) hCommon).
let p.
assume hp hPExtremal.
claim hValXIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p x :e omega.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero).
claim hValYIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p y :e omega.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp y hy hPID hPExtremal hyNonzero).
claim hValZIn : extremal_valuation K add mul p z :e omega.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp z hz hPID hPExtremal hzNonzero).
claim hValZLeX : extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_monotone_under_divisibility
K add mul p hp z hz x hx hPID hPExtremal
hzNonzero hxNonzero hZDividesX).
claim hValZLeY : extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
extremal_valuation K add mul p y.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_monotone_under_divisibility
K add mul p hp z hz y hy hPID hPExtremal
hzNonzero hyNonzero hZDividesY).
exact (god1_natural_minimum_greatest_lower_bound
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x) hValXIn
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y) hValYIn
(extremal_valuation K add mul p z) hValZIn
hValZLeX hValZLeY).
- assume hBounds.
claim hZDividesX : ring_divides K mul z x.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_bounds_imply_divisibility
K add mul z hz x hx hPID hzNonzero hxNonzero
(fun p hp hPExtremal =>
Subq_tra
(extremal_valuation K add mul p z)
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(hBounds p hp hPExtremal)
(andER
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y) :e omega)
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(andEL
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y) :e omega
/\ natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(god1_natural_minimum_in_and_bounds
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp y hy hPID hPExtremal hyNonzero)))))).
claim hZDividesY : ring_divides K mul z y.
exact (god1_extremal_valuation_bounds_imply_divisibility
K add mul z hz y hy hPID hzNonzero hyNonzero
(fun p hp hPExtremal =>
Subq_tra
(extremal_valuation K add mul p z)
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(hBounds p hp hPExtremal)
(andER
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y) :e omega
/\ natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
c= extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(god1_natural_minimum_in_and_bounds
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp x hx hPID hPExtremal hxNonzero)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)
(god1_extremal_valuation_in
K add mul p hp y hy hPID hPExtremal hyNonzero))))).
exact (andI
(ring_divides K mul z x)
(ring_divides K mul z y)
hZDividesX hZDividesY).
Qed.

Theorem god1_hcf_and_lcm_by_extremal_valuations :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y d m :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
<-> d <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p d
= natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
/\ (least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m
<-> m <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p m
= natural_maximum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy.
let d.
assume hd.
let m.
assume hm hPID hxne hyne.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists q :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul q)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
//GOD1PRF:957992 Given two non-zero elements $x, y$ of K , it is easy to construct their h.c.f. and l.c.m. with the aid of Lemma 4. Let $d$ be an h.c.f. of $x$ and $y$; then we have to express that the divisors of $x$ and $y$ are the divisors of $d$. Now the common divisors of $x$ and $y$ are, by Lemma 4, the elements $z \in \mathrm{~K}$ which satisfy
claim h_s31_valuation_l4_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set, forall x0 y0 :e K0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
x0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 -> y0 <> ring_zero K0 add0 ->
(ring_divides K0 mul0 x0 y0
<-> forall p0 :e K0, extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 p0 ->
extremal_valuation K0 add0 mul0 p0 x0 c=
extremal_valuation K0 add0 mul0 p0 y0).
apply god1_s31_lemma4_divisibility_by_extremal_valuations.
claim h_s31_hcf_common_divisor_valuations : forall z :e K,
z <> ring_zero K add ->
((ring_divides K mul z x /\ ring_divides K mul z y)
<-> forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y)).
exact (fun z hz hzNonzero =>
god1_common_divisor_iff_extremal_valuation_minimum_bound
K add mul x hx y hy z hz hPID hxne hyne hzNonzero).
//GOD1PRF:958401 that is,
claim h_s31_hcf_valuation_bound : forall z :e K,
ring_divides K mul z x -> ring_divides K mul z y ->
forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
let z.
assume hz hZDividesX hZDividesY.
claim hzNonzero : z <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_nonzero_multiple_has_nonzero_divisor
K add mul hRing z hz x hx hxne hZDividesX).
exact (iffEL
(ring_divides K mul z x /\ ring_divides K mul z y)
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p z c=
natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
(h_s31_hcf_common_divisor_valuations z hz hzNonzero)
(andI
(ring_divides K mul z x)
(ring_divides K mul z y)
hZDividesX hZDividesY)).
//GOD1PRF:958683 for all $p \in \mathrm{P}$. For $d$ to be an h.c.f. of $x$ and $y$, it is therefore necessary and sufficient that the conditions (10) and (11) should be equivalent, or in other words that
claim h_s31_hcf_valuation_characterization :

(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)

//GOD1PRF:958891 v_{p}(d)=\min \left(v_{p}(x), v_{p}(y)\right) \quad \text { for all } p \in \mathrm{P} . \tag{12}

claim h_s31_lcm_max_formula :

(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m ->
forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p m

(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y).
assume hLcm.
exact (andER
(m <> ring_zero K add)
(forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p m
= natural_maximum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
(iffEL
(least_common_multiple K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) m)
(m <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p m
= natural_maximum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
h_s31_lcm_valuation_characterization hLcm)).
exact (andI
(highest_common_factor K add mul 2
(fun i => if i = 0 then x else y) d
<-> d <> ring_zero K add
/\ forall p :e K, extremal_element K add mul p ->
extremal_valuation K add mul p d
= natural_minimum
(extremal_valuation K add mul p x)
(extremal_valuation K add mul p y))
