Theorem god1_fraction_class_member :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall a b :e K, b <> ring_zero K add ->
fraction_class K add mul (a,b) :e fraction_field K add mul.
let K add mul a.
assume ha.
let b.
assume hb hbNonzero.
exact (ReplI
(fraction_pairs K add) (fraction_class K add mul)
(a,b)
(god1_fraction_pair_intro K add a ha b hb hbNonzero)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_module_finitely_supported_sum_natural_successor :
forall G, forall op:set -> set -> set,
abelian_group G op -> forall n :e omega, forall f:set -> set,
(forall i :e ordsucc n, f i :e G) ->
module_finitely_supported_sum G op (ordsucc n) f
= op (module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f) (f n).
let G op.
assume hAbelian.
let n.
assume hn.
let f.
assume hMaps.
claim hPrefixMaps : forall i :e n, f i :e G.
exact (fun i hi => hMaps i (ordsuccI1 n i hi)).
claim hSuccessorToFinite :
module_finitely_supported_sum G op (ordsucc n) f
= ring_finite_sum G op (ordsucc n) f.
exact (god1_module_finitely_supported_sum_finite_index
G op hAbelian (ordsucc n)
(nat_finite (ordsucc n)
(nat_ordsucc n (omega_nat_p n hn)))
f hMaps).
claim hPrefixToFinite :
module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f
= ring_finite_sum G op n f.
exact (god1_module_finitely_supported_sum_finite_index
G op hAbelian n (nat_finite n (omega_nat_p n hn))
f hPrefixMaps).
exact (eq_i_tra
(module_finitely_supported_sum G op (ordsucc n) f)
(ring_finite_sum G op (ordsucc n) f)
(op (module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f) (f n))
hSuccessorToFinite
(eq_i_tra
(ring_finite_sum G op (ordsucc n) f)
(op (ring_finite_sum G op n f) (f n))
(op (module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f) (f n))
(god1_ring_finite_sum_natural_successor G op n hn f)
(f_eq_i (fun z => op z (f n))
(ring_finite_sum G op n f)
(module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f)
(eq_sym
(module_finitely_supported_sum G op n f)
(ring_finite_sum G op n f) hPrefixToFinite)))).
Qed.

Theorem god1_fraction_two_denominator_bezout_split :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul ->
forall a b1 b2 u v :e K,
b1 <> ring_zero K add -> b2 <> ring_zero K add ->
add (mul u b2) (mul v b1) = ring_one K mul ->
fraction_class K add mul (a,mul b1 b2)
= fraction_addition K add mul
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a u,b1))
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a v,b2)).
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
claim hComm : commutative_on K mul.
exact (andER (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let a.
assume ha.
let b1.
assume hb1.
let b2.
assume hb2.
let u.
assume hu.
let v.
assume hv hb1Nonzero hb2Nonzero hBezout.
claim hAU : mul a u :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing a ha u hu).
claim hAV : mul a v :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing a ha v hv).
claim hBProduct : mul b1 b2 :e K.
exact (god1_ring_multiplicative_law K add mul hRing
b1 hb1 b2 hb2).
claim hBProductNonzero : mul b1 b2 <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_nonzero_product
K add mul hIntegral b1 hb1 b2 hb2 hb1Nonzero hb2Nonzero).
claim hPair1 : (mul a u,b1) :e fraction_pairs K add.
exact (god1_fraction_pair_intro K add
(mul a u) hAU b1 hb1 hb1Nonzero).
claim hPair2 : (mul a v,b2) :e fraction_pairs K add.
exact (god1_fraction_pair_intro K add
(mul a v) hAV b2 hb2 hb2Nonzero).
claim hTotalPair : (a,mul b1 b2) :e fraction_pairs K add.
exact (god1_fraction_pair_intro K add
a ha (mul b1 b2) hBProduct hBProductNonzero).
claim hAdditionFormula :
fraction_addition K add mul
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a u,b1))
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a v,b2))
= fraction_class K add mul
(add (mul (mul a u) b2) (mul b1 (mul a v)),
mul b1 b2).
claim hRawAddition :
(fraction_addition K add mul
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a u,b1))
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a v,b2))
= fraction_class K add mul
(add
(mul ((mul a u,b1) 0) ((mul a v,b2) 1))
(mul ((mul a u,b1) 1) ((mul a v,b2) 0)),
mul ((mul a u,b1) 1) ((mul a v,b2) 1))).
exact (andEL
(fraction_addition K add mul
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a u,b1))
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a v,b2))
= fraction_class K add mul
(add
(mul ((mul a u,b1) 0) ((mul a v,b2) 1))
(mul ((mul a u,b1) 1) ((mul a v,b2) 0)),
mul ((mul a u,b1) 1) ((mul a v,b2) 1)))
(fraction_multiplication K add mul
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a u,b1))
(fraction_class K add mul (mul a v,b2))
= fraction_class K add mul
(mul ((mul a u,b1) 0) ((mul a v,b2) 0),
mul ((mul a u,b1) 1) ((mul a v,b2) 1)))
(god1_fraction_class_operation_formulas

assume ha.

Theorem god1_partial_fraction_pairwise_coprime_successor_family :

coprime_elements K add mul (b i) (b j)) ->
exists c :e K :^: ordsucc m,
fraction_class K add mul
(a,ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc m) (fun i => b i))
= module_finitely_supported_sum
(fraction_field K add mul) (fraction_addition K add mul) (ordsucc m)
(fun i => fraction_class K add mul (c i,b i)).

assume hPID.

coprime_elements K add mul (b i) (b j)) ->
exists c :e K :^: ordsucc 0,
fraction_class K add mul
(a,ring_finite_product K add mul (ordsucc 0) (fun i => b i))
= module_finitely_supported_sum
(fraction_field K add mul) (fraction_addition K add mul) (ordsucc 0)
(fun i => fraction_class K add mul (c i,b i)).

assume ha.
let b.
assume hb hNonzero hPairwise.

(fraction_field K add mul) (fraction_addition K add mul) (ordsucc m)

(module_finitely_supported_sum
(fraction_field K add mul) (fraction_addition K add mul) (ordsucc m)
(fun i => fraction_class K add mul (c0 i,b i)))
hRestrictedEquation hSumCong)))).
exact (god1_partial_fraction_extend_coprime_last

hNonzero hPairwise hPrefixInduction).
claim hAll : forall q, nat_p q ->

Theorem god1_integral_domain_natural_power_nonzero :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
integral_domain K add mul -> forall x :e K,
x <> ring_zero K add -> forall n :e omega,
ring_nat_power K add mul x n <> ring_zero K add.
let K add mul.
assume hIntegral.
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let x.
assume hx hxNonzero.
claim hOneNonzero : ring_one K mul <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_one_ne_zero K add mul hIntegral).
claim hBase : ring_nat_power K add mul x 0 <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => z <> ring_zero K add)
(ring_one K mul) (ring_nat_power K add mul x 0)
(eq_sym
(ring_nat_power K add mul x 0) (ring_one K mul)
(god1_ring_nat_power_zero K add mul x))
hOneNonzero).
claim hStep : forall m, nat_p m ->
ring_nat_power K add mul x m <> ring_zero K add ->
ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc m) <> ring_zero K add.
let m.
assume hm hInduction.
claim hmOmega : m :e omega.
exact (nat_p_omega m hm).
claim hPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x m :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx m hmOmega).
claim hProductNonzero :
mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x m) x <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_nonzero_product
K add mul hIntegral
(ring_nat_power K add mul x m) hPowerIn x hx
hInduction hxNonzero).
exact (god1_predicate_eq_subst
(fun z => z <> ring_zero K add)
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x m) x)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc m))
(eq_sym
(ring_nat_power K add mul x (ordsucc m))
(mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x m) x)
(god1_ring_nat_power_successor K add mul x m hm))
hProductNonzero).
let n.
assume hn.
exact (nat_ind
(fun m => ring_nat_power K add mul x m <> ring_zero K add)
hBase hStep n (omega_nat_p n hn)).
Qed.

Theorem god1_coprime_element_positive_natural_power :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,

principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->

let y.

exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).

(ring_nat_power K add mul y (ordsucc 0)).

y (ring_nat_power K add mul y (ordsucc 0))

hCoprime).

coprime_elements K add mul x
(ring_nat_power K add mul y (ordsucc (ordsucc m))).

hBase hStep).

Theorem god1_coprime_positive_natural_powers :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall x y :e K,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
x <> ring_zero K add -> y <> ring_zero K add ->
coprime_elements K add mul x y ->
forall r s :e omega, 0 :e r -> 0 :e s ->
coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s).
let K add mul x.
assume hx.
let y.
assume hy hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hCoprime.
claim hIntegral : integral_domain K add mul.
exact (andEL
(integral_domain K add mul)
(forall I,
two_sided_ideal K add mul I ->
exists d :e K, I = principal_ideal K add mul d)
hPID).
claim hCommRing : commutative_ring K add mul.
exact (god1_integral_domain_commutative_ring K add mul hIntegral).
claim hRing : ring K add mul.
exact (andEL (ring K add mul) (commutative_on K mul) hCommRing).
let r.
assume hr.
let s.
assume hs hrPositive hsPositive.
claim hXPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul x r :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing x hx r hr).
claim hYPowerIn : ring_nat_power K add mul y s :e K.
exact (god1_ring_nat_power_in K add mul hRing y hy s hs).
claim hYPowerNonzero :
ring_nat_power K add mul y s <> ring_zero K add.
exact (god1_integral_domain_natural_power_nonzero
K add mul hIntegral y hy hyNonzero s hs).
claim hXWithYPower : coprime_elements K add mul x
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s).
exact (god1_coprime_element_positive_natural_power
K add mul x hx y hy hPID hxNonzero hyNonzero hCoprime
s hs hsPositive).
claim hYPowerWithX : coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s) x.
exact (iffEL
(coprime_elements K add mul x (ring_nat_power K add mul y s))
(coprime_elements K add mul (ring_nat_power K add mul y s) x)
(god1_coprime_elements_symmetric
K add mul x hx (ring_nat_power K add mul y s) hYPowerIn hPID)
hXWithYPower).
claim hYPowerWithXPower : coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r).
exact (god1_coprime_element_positive_natural_power
K add mul (ring_nat_power K add mul y s) hYPowerIn
x hx hPID hYPowerNonzero hxNonzero hYPowerWithX
r hr hrPositive).
exact (iffER
(coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r)
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s))
(coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s)
(ring_nat_power K add mul x r))
(god1_coprime_elements_symmetric
K add mul (ring_nat_power K add mul x r) hXPowerIn
(ring_nat_power K add mul y s) hYPowerIn hPID)
hYPowerWithXPower).
Qed.

Theorem god1_s31_lemma6_powers_of_nonassociated_extremals_are_coprime :
forall K, forall add mul:set -> set -> set,
forall n :e omega, forall p :e K :^: n, forall r :e omega :^: n,
principal_ideal_domain K add mul ->
(forall i :e n, extremal_element K add mul (p i) /\ 0 :e r i) ->
(forall i j :e n, i <> j ->
not (associated_elements K add mul (p i) (p j))) ->
forall i j :e n, i <> j ->
coprime_elements K add mul
(ring_nat_power K add mul (p i) (r i))
(ring_nat_power K add mul (p j) (r j)).
let K add mul.
let n.
assume hn.
let p.
assume hp.

//GOD1PRF:961880 In other words, every element of $F$ can be written as a sum of fractions of the form $a / p^{n}$, where $a \in \mathrm{~K}, p \in \mathrm{~K}$ is extremal, and $n \geqslant 0$.

//GOD1PRF:962229 Theorem 8 is an immediate consequence of the following two lemmas :\\
claim h_s31_t8_lemma5_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall n0 :e omega, forall a0 :e K0, forall b0 :e K0 :^: n0,
0 :e n0 ->
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
(forall i :e n0, b0 i <> ring_zero K0 add0) ->
(forall i j :e n0, i <> j ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0 (b0 i) (b0 j)) ->
exists c0 :e K0 :^: n0,
fraction_class K0 add0 mul0
(a0,ring_finite_product K0 add0 mul0 n0 (fun i => b0 i))
= module_finitely_supported_sum
(fraction_field K0 add0 mul0) (fraction_addition K0 add0 mul0) n0
(fun i => fraction_class K0 add0 mul0 (c0 i,b0 i)).
apply god1_s31_lemma5_partial_fraction_coprime_denominators.
claim h_s31_t8_lemma6_formal_call :
forall K0, forall add0 mul0:set -> set -> set,
forall n0 :e omega, forall p0 :e K0 :^: n0, forall r0 :e omega :^: n0,
principal_ideal_domain K0 add0 mul0 ->
(forall i :e n0, extremal_element K0 add0 mul0 (p0 i) /\ 0 :e r0 i) ->
(forall i j :e n0, i <> j ->
not (associated_elements K0 add0 mul0 (p0 i) (p0 j))) ->
forall i j :e n0, i <> j ->
coprime_elements K0 add0 mul0
(ring_nat_power K0 add0 mul0 (p0 i) (r0 i))
(ring_nat_power K0 add0 mul0 (p0 j) (r0 j)).
apply god1_s31_lemma6_powers_of_nonassociated_extremals_are_coprime.
exact h_s31_t8_partial_fraction_form.
Qed.
